<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1729 Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 9 Ramadan 1446 H - March 9, 2025 G
2 A
</header>
# Ministry of Justice
## Announcement
On the occasion of the issuance of the decision by the Bankruptcy Judge / Zaid Al-Attar <orig>زيد العطار</orig> dated 17/2/2025 in Petition No. (23/2024) Declaration of Bankruptcy.
Submitted by / The Insurance Regulatory Unit.
Against / Ghazal Insurance Company <orig>شركة غزال للتأمين</orig>.
We hereby publish the aforementioned decision of the Bankruptcy Judge in the Official Gazette.
Head of the Bankruptcy Department
In the name of His Highness the Amir of the State of Kuwait
Sheikh Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>الشيخ مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>
Court of First Instance
Decision
On Monday, 17/2/2025, at the headquarters of the Bankruptcy Department
With the membership of Mr. / Zaid Abdul Hadi Al-Attar <orig>زيد عبد الهادي العطار</orig>, Bankruptcy Judge
And in the presence of Mr. / Khalid Abdullah Al-Qaisi <orig>خالد عبد الله القيسي</orig>, Secretary
In Petition No: (23/2024 Declaration of Bankruptcy)
Registered under automated number: 240825520
Submitted by: The Insurance Regulatory Unit
Against/ Ghazal Insurance Company <orig>شركة غزال للتأمين</orig>
After reviewing the documents and the trustee's letter requesting permission to open the portal for claims electronically and to approve a nominal, non-refundable fee to cover the costs of the process, and in accordance with the provisions of the Bankruptcy Law and its executive regulations:
The facts of the present petition are encompassed by the Bankruptcy Judge's decision issued on 26/6/2024, accepting the petition and initiating the bankruptcy declaration procedures against Ghazal Insurance Company <orig>شركة غزال للتأمين</orig>, setting the petition submission date of 29/2/2024 as a temporary date for the cessation of payments, and appointing the trustee to perform the tasks contained therein, to which we refer to avoid repetition.
Whereas, as stipulated in Article (105) of the Bankruptcy Law, "The Bankruptcy Department shall notify the trustee of the decision for their appointment within ten days from the date of its issuance, and it must provide them with all available information about the debtor. The debtor, within ten days from the date of being notified of the appointment decision, must do the following:
1- Announce a summary of the decision to initiate the procedures, provided that the announcement includes an invitation to creditors to submit their claims and supporting documents and deliver them to the trustee within a period not exceeding one month from the date of the announcement.
2- Notify all creditors whose electronic addresses are known to provide the trustee with their claims and documents within one month from the date of the announcement of the summary of the decision to initiate procedures. The debtor must provide the trustee with any additional details not previously notified to the Bankruptcy Department, whether regarding their creditors, the amounts of debts, details of any contracts under execution, or any pending or ongoing judicial proceedings to which the debtor is a party, within the timeframe specified by the trustee."
Guided by the foregoing, and as the trustee has requested permission to open the portal for claims electronically due to the impossibility of manually compiling them given their vast quantity, and to approve a nominal fee for submitting the claim to cover the costs of the process self-sufficiently without burdening the bankruptcy estate with any additional charges for a period of three months from the date of publishing the decision in the Official Gazette, renewable; and whereas Article (105) of the Bankruptcy Law has specified a period of one month, starting from the date of the announcement, for creditors to submit their claims and supporting documents and deliver them to the trustee, we therefore decide to open the portal for claims electronically for a period of one month from the date of publishing and announcing this decision in the Official Gazette, with the approval of a nominal, non-refundable fee to cover the costs of the process.
Therefore, we have decided:
1- To open the portal for claims electronically for a period of one month from the date of publishing and announcing this decision in the Official Gazette, with the approval of a nominal, non-refundable fee to cover the costs of the process.
2- The Bankruptcy Department shall provide the trustee with a true copy of this decision, publish and announce it in the Official Gazette, and legally notify the concerned parties thereof.
Secretary
Bankruptcy Judge
In accordance with Article (8) of the Bankruptcy Law, decisions issued by the Bankruptcy Judge are executory instruments according to this law. The Bankruptcy Department shall affix the writ of execution to them, and they shall be enforceable immediately upon issuance and without announcement.

# Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
## Ministerial Resolution No. (20) of 2025
### Concerning the formation of a committee to follow up on the implementation of the Smart License project

**The Minister of Commerce and Industry,**

**Having reviewed:**
- Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979 regarding the Supervision of Trade in Goods, Services, and Crafts, and its amendments,
- And Decree-Law No. (15) of 1979 concerning the Civil Service, and its amending laws,
- And Decree-Law No. (68) of 1980 issuing the Commercial Law, and its amending laws,
- And Law No. 63 of 1982 concerning the establishment of the Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig>, and its amending laws,
- And Law No. 94 of 1983 establishing the Public Authority for Agriculture Affairs and Fish Resources <orig>الهيئة العامة لشئون الزراعة والثروة السمكية</orig>, and its amending laws,
- And Law No. 56 of 1996 concerning the issuance of the Industry Law, and its amending laws,
- And Law No. 22 of 2009 concerning the approval of the Unified Industrial Regulation (System) for the Gulf Cooperation Council (GCC) states,
- And Law No. 7 of 2010 concerning the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, and its amending laws,
- And Law No. 111 of 2013 concerning Commercial Shop Licenses,
- And Law No. 109 of 2013 concerning the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>,
- And Law No. 112 of 2013 establishing the Public Authority for Food and Nutrition <orig>الهيئة العامة للغذاء والتغذية</orig>,
- And Law No. 37 of 2014 establishing the Communication and Information Technology Regulatory Authority <orig>هيئة تنظيم الاتصالات وتقنية المعلومات</orig>, as amended by Law No. 98 of 2015,
- And Law No. 1 of 2016 issuing the Companies Law, and its amending laws,
- Law No. 33 of 2016 concerning Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>, as amended by Law No. 1 of 2018,
- And Law No. (18) of 2018 concerning the Commercial Register,
- And Law No. (125) of 2019 concerning the Regulation of Insurance,
- And Law No. (13) of 2020 concerning the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>,
- And the Decree issued on April 4, 1979, concerning the Civil Service System, and its amending decrees,
- And the Decree issued on January 7, 1979, concerning the Ministry of Information <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>,
- And the Decree issued on January 7, 1979, concerning the Ministry of Public Health <orig>وزارة الصحة العامة</orig>,
- And the Decree issued on January 7, 1979, concerning the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>,
- And the Decree issued on January 7, 1979, concerning the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>,
- And Decree No. (191) of 2015 concerning the organization of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>,
- And Decree No. (50) of 2017 concerning the Ministry of Social Affairs <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية</orig>,
- And Decree No. 73 of 2024 on the formation of the Cabinet, and its amending decrees,
- And upon the proposal of the Undersecretary of the Ministry,
- And based on the requirements of the public interest,
- And pursuant to the powers vested in us.

**Has decided**

### Article (1)
A committee shall be formed to follow up on the implementation of the Smart License project, chaired by the Undersecretary of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, Mr. Ziad Abdullah Al-Najem <orig>زياد عبد الله الناجم</orig>, with the membership of representatives from the concerned authorities, whose grade shall not be less than that of a Department Director or its equivalent.
1- A representative from Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>
2- A representative from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
3- A representative from the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>
4- A representative from the Public Authority for Food and Nutrition <orig>الهيئة العامة للغذاء والتغذية</orig>
5- A representative from the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>
6- A representative from the Ministry of Information <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>
7- A representative from the Communication and Information Technology Regulatory Authority <orig>هيئة تنظيم الاتصالات وتقنية المعلومات</orig>
8- A representative from the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>
9- A representative from the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
10- A representative from the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
11- A representative from the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>
12- A representative from the Ministry of Higher Education <orig>وزارة التعليم العالي</orig>
13- A representative from the Ministry of Social Affairs <orig>وزارة الشؤون الاجتماعية</orig>
14- A representative from the Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig>
15- A representative from the Public Authority for Agriculture Affairs and Fish Resources <orig>الهيئة العامة لشؤون الزراعة والثروة السمكية</orig>
16- A representative from the Direct Investment Promotion Authority <orig>هيئة تشجيع الاستثمار المباشر</orig>
17- A representative from the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>
18- A representative from the Insurance Regulatory Unit <orig>وحدة تنظيم التأمين</orig>
# Ministry of Higher Education <orig>وزارة التعليم العالي</orig>
## Ministerial Resolution No. (63/2025)
Concerning the addition of certain academic programs and degrees to the list of higher education institutions approved for enrollment in bachelor's and postgraduate programs in the United Arab Emirates.
<page_end>3</page_end>

<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1729 Seventy-First Year 41
Sunday, 9 Ramadan 1446 H – 9/3/2025 G
</header>



- Having reviewed Decree-Law No. 15 of 1979 concerning the Civil Service and its amending laws.
- And the Decree issued on April 4, 1979, concerning the Civil Service System and its amendments.
- And Amiri Decree No. (417) of 2010 issued on October 25, 2010, concerning the establishment of the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig>.
- And Ministerial Resolution No. (272) issued on October 3, 2012, concerning allowing Kuwaiti students to enroll for study outside the State of Kuwait only in universities for which a ministerial resolution is issued by the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig>.
- And Academic Decision No. (2014/32) dated July 8, 2014, concerning the list of higher education institutions in which enrollment is permitted for bachelor's and postgraduate studies in the United Arab Emirates.
- And the decision of the Board of Directors of the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig> No. (7) issued on December 31, 2014, which includes the mechanism for issuing decisions related to identifying higher education institutions outside the State of Kuwait whose graduates' qualifications are permitted for accreditation.
- And the decision of the Board of Directors of the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig> No. (2014/5) concerning the determination of criteria for selecting higher education institutions outside the State of Kuwait.
- And based on the letter from the Cultural Office in Dubai No. (M.Th.D/97/2025) dated January 16, 2025.
- And based on the recommendation of the Committee for Proposing Standards and Reviewing and Updating Lists of Higher Education Institutions Outside the State of Kuwait in its second meeting held on February 6, 2025.

And any other entity the Committee deems necessary to involve in the implementation and follow-up of the project.

## Article (2)
The Committee shall undertake the following tasks:
- Implementing the Smart License project.
- Coordinating among the concerned authorities to ensure the effective implementation of the project's phases.
- Following up on the project's implementation according to the approved plan and ensuring its objectives are achieved.
- Developing the executive plan and timeline to ensure work proceeds according to the specified phases.
- Reviewing the legal frameworks and proposing the necessary legislative amendments to support the project's implementation.
- Continuous coordination with the concerned authorities to ensure integration among the various related entities.
- Preparing the training requirements in cooperation with the implementing company to ensure the project's operational readiness.
- Preparing and submitting periodic reports to the Minister of Commerce to evaluate the implementation phases and make the necessary decisions.
- Any other competencies added by the Minister.

## Article (3)
The Committee shall establish the system it deems appropriate to organize its work, and it may, in the course of carrying out its tasks, seek the assistance of any experts or specialized bodies it deems necessary to achieve its objectives to the fullest extent.

## Article (4)
The team's term of work shall be six months, starting from the date of issuance of this decision. It may be extended for a similar period upon a request from the Committee's chairman via an official letter, subject to the Minister's approval. None of the Committee members shall be entitled to any financial remuneration for their participation in its work.

## Article (5)
This decision shall come into effect from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette. The concerned authorities shall implement its provisions, each within its own jurisdiction.

Minister of Commerce and Industry
Khalifa Abdullah Al-Ajil <orig>خليفة عبد الله العجيل</orig>

Issued on: 25 Sha'ban 1446 H
Corresponding to: February 24, 2025 G

  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains two official decisions: one from the Ministry of Education approving a PhD program in Quranic studies at the University of Sharjah, and another from the Ministry of Interior regarding the treatment of minor children of a Kuwaiti citizen and a Saudi national."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1729, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 9 Ramadan 1446 H – March 9, 2025 G
5 A
</header>


- And based on the public interest.

(It is decided)

### Article One
To add the PhD program in Tafsir and Quranic Sciences at the University of Sharjah to Academic Decision No. (32/2014) issued on July 8, 2014, which permits enrollment in undergraduate and postgraduate programs in the United Arab Emirates.

### Article Two
The study must be on a regular attendance basis during the academic week, and the academic program in which students enroll must follow the traditional education system.

### Article Three
The academic program in which students enroll must have completed the specified duration for awarding the degree, with the graduation of the first cohort from the college offering this program.

### Article Four
The decisions regulating enrollment and the system of study in educational institutions outside the State of Kuwait must be observed. It must also be ensured that the academic degrees have met the requirements for their attainment in accordance with the regulating decisions issued by the Ministry of Higher Education <orig>وزارة التعليم العالي</orig> in the State of Kuwait.

### Article Five
This decision shall take effect from its date, and any provision that contradicts what is stated in this decision shall be repealed. It shall be published in the Official Gazette.

### Article Six
The competent authorities shall be informed and act accordingly.

Minister of Higher Education and Scientific Research
Prof. Dr. Nader Abdullah Mohammed Al-Jalal <orig>نادر عبد الله محمد الجلال</orig>

Issued on: 24 Sha'ban 1446 H
Corresponding to: February 23, 2025 G

---

# Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
## (Decision No. 712 of 2025)
### Regarding: Treatment of Minors

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Interior
- Having reviewed Amiri Decree No. 15 of 1959 concerning the Kuwaiti Nationality Law and its amending laws.
- And on Ministerial Decision No. 94/2024 regarding the delegation of certain powers.
- And on the letter from the General Department of Nationality and Kuwaiti Travel Documents <orig>الإدارة العامة للجنسية ووثائق السفر الكويتية</orig> No. 1373 dated January 26, 2025, and its attachments.

It is decided

### Article (1)
The minors listed below, children of the citizen/ Shamma Aloush Awad Al-Humaidi Al-Mutairi <orig>شما علوش عوض الحميدي المطيري</orig> from her divorcé/ Matash Saad Saud Al-Dosari <orig>معطش سعد سعود الدوسري</orig> – a Saudi national – shall be treated as Kuwaitis until they reach the age of majority. They are:
1- Asma Matash Saad Saud Al-Dosari <orig>أسماء معطش سعد سعود الدوسري</orig>, born in Kuwait on May 7, 2005.
2- Ali Matash Saad Saud Al-Dosari <orig>علي معطش سعد سعود الدوسري</orig>, born in Kuwait on October 16, 2006.
3- Saud Matash Saad Saud Al-Dosari <orig>سعود معطش سعد سعود الدوسري</orig>, born in Kuwait on December 13, 2009.

### Article (2)
The concerned parties shall implement this decision, and it shall take effect from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette.

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Interior
Lieutenant General
Salem Nawaf Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>سالم نواف الأحمد الصباح</orig>

Issued on: 24 Sha'ban 1446 H
Corresponding to: February 23, 2025 G

**Has Decided**

### Article (1)
The minor, Saleh Ahmed Osama Mohammed Bandari <orig>صالح أحمد أسامه محمد بنداري</orig>, born in Kuwait on March 27, 2009, son of the citizen, Sarah Saleh Abdullah Saleh Nasser <orig>ساره صالح عبدالله صالح ناصر</orig>, from her divorcé, Ahmed Osama Mohammed Bandari <orig>أحمد أسامه محمد بنداري</orig>, of Egyptian nationality, shall be treated as a Kuwaiti until he reaches the age of majority.

### Article (2)
All concerned parties shall implement this decision, and it shall come into effect from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette.

**Undersecretary of the Ministry of Interior**
**Lieutenant General**
**Salem Nawaf Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>سالم نواف الأحمد الصباح</orig>**

# (Decision No. 714 of 2025)
## Regarding: Treatment of Minors

**Undersecretary of the Ministry of Interior**

- Having reviewed Amiri Decree No. 15/59 concerning the Kuwaiti Nationality Law and its amending laws.
- And upon Ministerial Decision No. 94/2024 regarding the delegation of certain competencies.
- And upon the letter from the General Department of Nationality and Kuwaiti Travel Documents <orig>الإدارة العامة للجنسية ووثائق السفر الكويتية</orig> No. 1384 dated January 26, 2025, and its attachments.

**Has Decided**

### Article (1)
The two minors named below, children of the citizen, Suad Rahil Rahi Hussein Hazaa Al-Fadhli <orig>سعاد رحيل راهي حسين هزاع الفضلي</orig>, from her divorcé, Fahad Abdullah Hussein Hazaa <orig>فهد عبدالله حسين هزاع</orig>, a non-Kuwaiti, shall be treated as Kuwaitis until they reach the age of majority. They are:
1- Sarah Fahad Abdullah Hussein Hazaa <orig>ساره فهد عبدالله حسين هزاع</orig>, born in Kuwait on January 26, 2005 AD
2- Abdullah Fahad Abdullah Hussein Hazaa <orig>عبدالله فهد عبدالله حسين هزاع</orig>, born in Kuwait on July 19, 2006 AD

### Article (2)
All concerned parties shall implement this decision, and it shall come into effect from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette.

**Undersecretary of the Ministry of Interior**
**Lieutenant General**
**Salem Nawaf Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>سالم نواف الأحمد الصباح</orig>**

Issued on: 24 Sha'ban 1446 AH
Corresponding to: February 23, 2025 AD

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1729, Seventy-first Year | Sunday, 9 Ramadan 1446 AH - March 9, 2025 AD | 71
</header>


- And upon Ministerial Resolution No. 94/2024 regarding the delegation of certain competencies.

**It is decided**

### Article (1)
The minor, Nasser Mohammed Nasser Hussein Al-Obaidli <orig>ناصر محمد ناصر حسين العبيدلي</orig>, born in Kuwait on February 11, 2013, son of the citizen Iman Mosaed Bilal Al-Abkal <orig>إيمان مساعد بلال العبكل</orig> from her divorcé Mohammed Nasser Hussein Al-Obaidli <orig>محمد ناصر حسين العبيدلي</orig>, of Emirati nationality, shall be treated as a Kuwaiti until he reaches the age of majority.

### Article (2)

**Undersecretary of the Ministry of Interior**
**Lieutenant General**

  ],
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",

<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1729 Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 9 Ramadan 1446 H - 9/3/2025 G
11
</header>


- And upon the Decree issued on 4/4/1979 regarding the Civil Service System and its amendments.
- And upon Decree No. (50) of 2017 concerning the Ministry of Social Affairs <orig>وزارة الشؤون الاجتماعية</orig>.
- And upon the Council of Ministers Decision No. (666) of 2001 concerning the regulation of the growth of organizational structures in ministries, government departments, and public bodies and institutions.
- And upon Ministerial Decision No. 93 of 1993 concerning the replanning, organization, and creation of administrative units in the Ministry.
- And upon Ministerial Decision No. 7 of 1994 concerning the determination of the organizational competencies of the administrative units in the Ministry and its amending ministerial decisions.
- And upon the Civil Service Commission <orig>ديوان الخدمة المدنية</orig> Circular No. 15 of 2001 concerning the regulation of the growth of organizational structures in ministries, government departments, and public bodies and institutions.
- And upon the letter of the Civil Service Commission <orig>ديوان الخدمة المدنية</orig> No. (2024097851) dated 12/1/2025 regarding the approval of amendments to the organizational structure.
- And after the presentation by the Undersecretary of the Ministry.
- And based on the requirements of the public interest.

### It is decided
### Article One
The "Coordination and Follow-up Department" shall be established, to be organizationally subordinate to the Assistant Undersecretary for Legal Affairs.

### Article Two
The Coordination and Follow-up Department shall exercise its duties through the following competencies:
- Preparing the department's annual work plan and presenting it to the Assistant Undersecretary of the sector, following up on its implementation after approval, and submitting periodic reports thereon.
- Providing technical and administrative supervision over the department's work, reviewing work in detail, and issuing the necessary directives to accomplish tasks in accordance with the required technical standards for the work.
- Working to overcome difficulties encountered in the department's work, providing necessary recommendations and suggestions to improve performance and develop work therein, and following up on the implementation of appropriate measures after their approval by the Assistant Undersecretary of the sector.
- Proposing the systems and regulations to be applied in the department and following up on their implementation and approval.

# Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>
## Ministerial Decision No. 119 of 2025

- The Minister of Justice:
- After reviewing the Constitution.
- And upon Decree-Law No. 38 of 1980 issuing the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law and its amendments.
- And upon Decree-Law No. 23 of 1990 concerning the Law on the Organization of the Judiciary and its amendments.
- And upon the decision of the Supreme Judicial Council <orig>المجلس الأعلى للقضاء</orig> in its session No. (7/2025) held on 16/2/2025.
- And upon joint coordination with all concerned parties.
- And as required by the public interest.

### It is decided
### Article One
All circuits of the Court of First Instance, the Court of Appeal, and the Court of Cassation shall be relocated from their current premises at the Justice Palace to their new premises located in the new Justice Palace building.

### Article Two
All circuits of the Capital Family Court – First Instance and Appeal – shall be relocated to the new Justice Palace building.

### Article Three
The relocation shall commence starting from Sunday, 9/3/2025.

### Article Four
The Undersecretary of the Ministry shall implement this decision in coordination with all concerned parties.

### Article Five
This decision shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>
Counselor / Nasser Yousef Al-Sumait <orig>ناصر يوسف السميط</orig>

Issued on: 3 Ramadan 1446 H
Corresponding to: 3 March 2025 G

- Coordination of joint work between the department and similar departments in the Ministry regarding the implementation of work related to the sector, within the limits of the applicable regulations and the powers granted to the department.
- Following up on responses to questions and inquiries received by the sector and preparing letters and memoranda regarding them in coordination with the Assistant Undersecretary for the sector and the concerned departments.
- Preparing for and following up on conferences, meetings, gatherings, media seminars, and other events attended or participated in by the Assistant Undersecretary for the sector.
- Following up on matters issued by the Assistant Undersecretary for the sector with the competent authorities inside and outside the Ministry and providing opinions on them in cooperation with the competent authorities.
- Following up on the implementation of decisions and recommendations related to the sector issued by the higher authorities in the Ministry, in coordination with the concerned authorities as directed by the Assistant Undersecretary for the sector, and submitting periodic reports on the follow-up results.
- Coordinating with the Ministry's sectors in responding to matters referred to the sector related to the work of specialized councils or any other official or private bodies.
- Following up on the application of job description cards for positions within the department, ensuring that all concerned employees understand the contents of these cards as they pertain to them, and coordinating with the concerned authorities to make necessary amendments whenever needed.
- Preparing a record of information on official or private entities related to the work of the Assistant Undersecretary for the sector.
- Identifying the training needs of the department in coordination with the competent authorities and the Assistant Undersecretary for the sector.
- Identifying the department's needs for administrative and technical staff in coordination with the concerned authorities and the Assistant Undersecretary for the sector.
- Preparing periodic and annual reports on the department's work and submitting them to the Assistant Undersecretary for the sector.

### Article Three
Any provision that contradicts the provisions of this decision shall be repealed.

### Article Four
The provisions of this decision shall be effective from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the competent authorities shall implement its contents.

Minister of Social Affairs
and Family and Childhood Affairs
Dr. Amthal Hadi Haif Al-Huwailah <orig>د. أمثال هادي هايف الحويلة</orig>

# Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
## Decision No. (36) of 2025
Regarding the removal of the late Mr. Abdul Latif Abdullah Hoshan Al-Majed from the special register of auditors

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, and its executive regulations and their amendments;
- And the auditor registration certificate of the late Mr. Abdul Latif Abdullah Hoshan Al-Majed <orig>عبداللطيف عبدالله هوشان الماجد</orig> No. (0019 / 2013 / EA) issued on 10/05/2022.
- And the death certificate issued by the Central Registry of Births and Deaths at the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> dated 13/01/2025.
- And based on Decision No. (04) of 2025 regarding the amendment of the final approval authorities for the work procedures of the Supervision Sector, issued on 12/01/2025.

The following has been decided

### Article One
The registration of the late Mr. Abdul Latif Abdullah Hoshan Al-Majed <orig>عبد اللطيف عبدالله هوشان الماجد</orig> shall be removed from the special register of auditors at the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>.

### Article Two
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Acting Head of the Supervision Sector
Fahad Abdullah Al-Fadhli <orig>فهد عبدالله الفضلي</orig>

Issued on: 06 March 2025 G

- And upon the decision of the Board of Directors of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig> No. (45/471/2023) issuing instructions for regulating electronic payment of funds.
- And based on the resolutions of the Ordinary General Assembly of the shareholders of the Shared Electronic Banking Services Company <orig>شركة الخدمات المصرفية الآلية المشتركة</orig> held on 26/12/2024.
- And upon the requests of the Shared Electronic Banking Services Company (Knet) <orig>شركة الخدمات المصرفية الآلية المشتركة (كي نت)</orig>, the last of which was on 5/1/2025, regarding the amendment of its data in the Register of Electronic Payment Service Providers, Electronic Money, and Operators of Electronic Payment Systems <orig>سجل مقدمو خدمات الدفع الإلكتروني والنقود الإلكترونية وتشغيل نظم الدفع الإلكتروني</orig> at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.

**It is decided**

**Article One**

The following amendments to the data of the Shared Electronic Banking Services Company (Knet) <orig>شركة الخدمات المصرفية الآلية المشتركة (كي نت)</orig> shall be noted in the Register of Electronic Payment Service Providers, Electronic Money, and Operators of Electronic Payment Systems <orig>سجل مقدمو خدمات الدفع الإلكتروني والنقود الإلكترونية وتشغيل نظم الدفع الإلكتروني</orig> at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>: (2/1)

1) Increasing the Mandatory Reserve <orig>الاحتياطي الإجباري</orig> balance from 500,100 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> to 1,144,314 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>. This is in accordance with the company's final financial statements for the fiscal year ending on 31/10/2024.
2) Reappointing Mrs. Sheikha Adnan Al-Fulaji <orig>شيخة عدنان الفليج</orig> from the office of Al-Aiban & Al-Osaimi & Partners (Ernst & Young) <orig>مكتب العيبان والعصيمي وشركاه (أرنست ويونغ)</orig> as the company's accounts auditor for the fiscal year ending on 31/10/2025.
3) Reappointing the members of the company's Sharia Supervisory Board <orig>هيئة الرقابة الشرعية</orig> for the fiscal year ending on 31/10/2025, as follows:
- Prof. Dr. Abdulaziz Al-Qassar <orig>عبدالعزيز القصار</orig>
- Prof. Dr. Ali Ibrahim Al-Rashed <orig>علي إبراهيم الراشد</orig>
- Prof. Dr. Essam Khalaf Al-Enezi <orig>عصام خلف العنزي</orig>

**Article Two**

This decision shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall be effective from the date of its issuance.

**The Governor**

Issued on: 21 Sha'ban 1446 H
Corresponding to: 20 February 2025 AD

Before concluding, the Chairman of the Board of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>رئيس مجلس الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> invited the honorable members of the Board to attend the next meeting.
The Agency's Board of Directors concluded its work at 11:30 PM.

The tender documents will be published on the Agency's website for review before proceeding to purchase the documents.
- The final time for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the announcement above for the submission of bids.
- Bidders and practitioners must adhere to the instructions for submitting and depositing bids on CD, which are available on the Agency's website WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW.
- The aforementioned fee is to be paid by a certified check or K-Net card.
- Companies/bidders wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must submit them to the concerned entity at the time and place specified in the table above for the preliminary meeting (inquiries session). Any inquiries or clarifications submitted to the Agency will not be considered.
- All documents must be submitted on a non-copiable CD, with the exception of the bid form and the initial bid bond, which must be submitted as hard copies.
- Not divisible.
- A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, must be submitted with the bid.
- The bidder must attach a valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there are no holds on the bidder's file.
- For government contracts registered with the Authority concerning one of the violations mentioned in Article 10 of Law No. 6 of 2010 regarding work in the private sector, it should be noted that bids not including this certificate will be disqualified.
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested bidders to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the bid-opening session.
- Companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the Bid Opening Department before the day scheduled for the bid-opening session and bring the following documents:
1. A copy of the Civil ID.
2. A copy of the signature authorization specific to the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
3. In the event that a person other than the authorized signatory attends, a written letter from the person whose signature is authorized with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> must be presented, delegating whomever they see fit to attend the session.
- Owners of small and medium enterprises are exempt from the fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to the Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016 <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة رقم 2016/49</orig>.
- Owners of small and medium enterprises wishing to apply for the tender must attach to their bid a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة و المتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
- This announcement is an integral part of the tender documents.
- For more information, please visit our website at WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW.
Secretary-General of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الأمين العام للجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>

## Announcement
The Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> announces the issuance of Tender No. WKM/38/2022/2023 for the maintenance of high-pressure lines up to 400 kV – Area One
Based on the request of the Ministry of Electricity, Water, and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>
The tender documents can be obtained from the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.

### Instructions
1- The Ministry must be notified of the names, positions, photos, and passports of the candidates attending the site visit seven days prior to its date. Submissions via fax will not be accepted.
2- The tender purchase receipt must be presented when attending the site visit and the preliminary meeting.

The tender documents will be published on the Agency's website for review before proceeding to purchase the documents.
- The final deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the announcement above for bid submission.
- Bidders and practitioners must adhere to the instructions for submitting and depositing bids on CD, which are available on the Agency's website: WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW
- The aforementioned fee is to be paid by a certified check or K-Net card.
- Companies/bidders wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must submit them to the concerned entity at the time and place specified in the schedule above for the preliminary meeting (Q&A session). Any inquiries or clarifications submitted to the Agency will not be considered.
- All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, with the exception of the bid form and the initial guarantee, which must be submitted as hard copies.
- Not divisible
- A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, must be submitted with the bid.
- The bidder must attach a valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there are no holds on the bidder's file for government contracts registered with the Authority due to any of the violations mentioned in Article 10 of Law No. 6 of 2010 regarding work in the private sector. Please note that bids not including this certificate will be disqualified.
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested bidders to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the bid opening session.
- Companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the Bid Opening Department before the day scheduled for the bid opening session and bring the following documents:
1. A copy of the Civil ID.
2. A copy of the signature authorization for the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.

3. In the event that a person other than the authorized signatory attends, a written letter from the person whose signature is authorized with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> must be provided, delegating whomever they see fit to attend the session.
- Owners of small and medium enterprises are exempt from the fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with the provisions of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to the Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016.
- Owners of small and medium enterprises wishing to apply for the tender must attach to their bid a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة و المتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
- This announcement is an integral part of the tender documents.
- For more information, please visit our website at WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW

**Secretary-General of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الأمين العام للجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>**

## Notice
Regarding Tender No. **RFP-2134156**
New Injection Network for Surplus Water in North Kuwait in the Sabriya / Bahra <orig>الصابرية / بحرة</orig> Area
**( SA / BA ) NEW NK INJECTION NETWORK FOR SA/BA AREA**
- Kuwait Oil Company (KOC) <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> -
The Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> would like to draw the attention of the esteemed bidders that a site visit for the locations of the aforementioned tender (North Kuwait area) will be conducted on 18-3-2025 and 19-3-2025 at 7:00 AM. Companies that have purchased the tender documents should send an email to (Ddoraei@kockw.com) and (FAQallaf@kockw.com) no later than 5 days after the site visit date. Please note that the gathering point will be at the Al-Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig> area, Al-Ahmadi Mega Complex Gate (2), Ahmadi, Kuwait.
This notice is hereby issued.
Secretary General of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الأمين العام للجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>

- The public tender documents will be published on CAPT’s website, for review prior to purchasing. Once the tender document fees been paid refund is not acceptable unless the tender is canceled in accordance with the provisions of Article (55) of the Public Tenders Law and its amendments.
- Closing date for submitting bids is no later than (1:00) PM of the tender announcement date.
- Bidders wishing to participate in this tender must abide by the CAPT’s instructions published on the CAPT’s website- www.capt.gov.kw
- Bids must be submitted on a compact disc (CD/ DVD) with (5) non-modifiable copies, with an exception to the form of tenders and the bid bond to be submitted as hard copies.
- indivisible.
- Tenders documents fees must be paid by certified cheque or Knet card.
- Inquiries and clarifications by bidders who paid the tender documents fees must be provided to the relevant public authority at the time and place specified above with a schedule for the pre-tender meeting (inquiry session), any inquiries or clarifications submitted directly to the CAPT will not be consider.
- A valid certificate of national manpower quota issued by the Public Authority for Manpower must be submitted with the bid, and a ‘To Whom It may concern certificate’ stating no hold applicable on the bidder file.

## Announcement

The owners of the company: Arleens for Snacks and Hot and Cold Beverages ## Company Under Liquidation
have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships at the Ministry to: Dissolve and liquidate the company.
Legal Entity: One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection should file a claim with the Court of First Instance within thirty days from the date of this announcement's publication, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The filing of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners (in the case of a general or simple limited partnership only) towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

# Kuwait Cement Company (K.S.C.P.)
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
Held on Wednesday, February 19, 2025

Upon the invitation of the Board of Directors of Kuwait Cement Company (K.S.C.P.), the Extraordinary General Assembly of the company's shareholders held its meeting at 10:30 AM on Wednesday, 02/19/2025, at the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry building (Bahra Hall – First Floor – Kuwait City), chaired by Mr. / Dr. Abdulaziz Rashed Al-Rashed <orig>د. عبد العزيز راشد الراشد</orig>, Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors.

The meeting was attended by:
- Mr. / Mohammed Al-Khudari <orig>محمد الخضري</orig>, representing the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> – Companies Department.
- Mr. / Mohammed Nasser Al-Subaie <orig>محمد ناصر السبيعي</orig>, representing the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.

After verifying and reviewing all invitations and proxies of the attendees, both in person and by proxy (in-person and electronic), the representative of the Kuwait Clearing Company announced that the legal quorum for convening the Extraordinary General Assembly was met with the attendance of shareholders representing 601,556,415 shares, equivalent to 84.373% of the company's net shares, which total 712,973,670 shares (after excluding treasury shares).

The Chairman of the Assembly opened the meeting by welcoming the attendees and then proceeded to review the items on the agenda. They were discussed as follows:

1- The Extraordinary General Assembly approved the amendment of the text of Article (18) of the company's Articles of Association, as follows:

<table_caption>Comparison of Article (18) Before and After Amendment</table_caption>
<table>
| Text Before Amendment | Text After Amendment |
| :--- | :--- |
| The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors composed of ten members, as follows:<br>1- Three members appointed by the Kuwait Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig>.<br>2- Two members appointed by the National Industries Group Holding (K.S.C.P.) <orig>مجموعة الصناعات الوطنية القابضة (ش م ك ع)</orig>.<br>3- One member appointed by Al-Rashed Company for Trading, Industry, and Contracting Ltd. <orig>شركة الراشد للتجارة والصناعة والمقاولات المحدودة</orig>.<br>4- Four members to be elected by secret ballot by the remaining shareholders. | The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors composed of ten members elected by the General Assembly through secret ballot.<br>Each shareholder, whether a natural or legal person, may appoint representatives to the company's Board of Directors in proportion to the shares they own. The number of Board members selected in this manner shall be deducted from the total number of Board members to be elected.<br>Shareholders who have representatives on the Board of Directors may not participate with other shareholders in electing the remaining members of the Board, except to the extent of their shareholding that exceeds the percentage used to appoint their representatives on the Board.<br>A group of shareholders may form an alliance among themselves to appoint one or more representatives to the Board of Directors in proportion to their combined ownership. These representatives shall have the same rights and duties as elected members, and the shareholder shall be responsible for the actions of their representatives towards the company, its creditors, and its shareholders.<br>It shall be taken into account that the majority of the Board of Directors members shall be non-executive members. Additionally, at least 20% of the Board of Directors members must be independent members, provided that their number does not exceed half of the Board members. It is not required for an independent member to be a shareholder in the company. |
</table>

The voting result for this item (representing 84.373% of the company's issued capital after excluding treasury shares) is as follows:
<table_caption>Voting Results for the Amendment of Article (18)</table_caption>
<table>
| Approved | Not Approved | Abstained |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 62.619% | 0% | 21.754% |
</table>

2- The Extraordinary General Assembly approved the amendment of the text of Article (19) of the Articles of Association, as follows:
<table_caption>Comparison of Article (19) Before and After Amendment</table_caption>
<table>
| Text Before Amendment | Text After Amendment |
| :--- | :--- |
| The term of the Board of Directors members is three years, renewable. | The term of the Board of Directors members is three years, renewable, starting from the date of the General Assembly's resolution to elect the Board members. A new Board of Directors shall be elected for a similar term immediately upon the expiration of the term of its predecessor. If there are serious reasons that make it impossible to hold elections on schedule, the current Board shall continue to manage the company until the date set by the Ministry for this purpose. |
</table>

The voting result for this item (representing 84.373% of the company's issued capital after excluding treasury shares) is as follows:
<table_caption>Voting Results for the Amendment of Article (19)</table_caption>
<table>
| Approved | Not Approved | Abstained |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 62.619% | 0% | 21.754% |
</table>

3- The Extraordinary General Assembly approved the amendment of the text of Article (22) of the Articles of Association, as follows:
<table_caption>Comparison of Article (22) Before and After Amendment</table_caption>
<table>
| Text Before Amendment | Text After Amendment |
| :--- | :--- |
| If a position of an elected Board member becomes vacant, it shall be filled by the shareholder who received the most votes among those who did not win membership in the last election. If they are unable to serve, the next in line shall succeed them, and so on. However, if the vacant positions reach half of the original positions, or if no one meets the conditions, the Board of Directors must call for a General Assembly meeting within two months from the date the last position became vacant to elect members to fill the vacant positions. This excludes members representing the Kuwait Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig>, the National Industries Group Holding (K.S.C.P.) <orig>مجموعة الصناعات الوطنية القابضة (ش م ك ع)</orig>, and Al-Rashed Company for Trading, Industry, and Contracting Ltd. <orig>شركة الراشد للتجارة والصناعة والمقاولات المحدودة</orig>. | If a position of an elected Board member becomes vacant, it shall be filled by the shareholder who received the most votes among those who did not win membership in the Board of Directors. If they are unable to serve, the next in line shall succeed them. However, if the vacant positions reach a quarter of the original positions, or if no one meets the conditions, the Board of Directors must call for an Ordinary General Assembly to convene within two months from the date the last position became vacant to elect members to fill the vacant positions, without prejudice to the right of shareholders who have representatives on the Board of Directors to appoint their successors if one of their positions becomes vacant during the term of membership. In all cases, the new member shall only complete the term of their predecessor. |
</table>

The voting result for this item (representing 84.373% of the company's issued capital after excluding treasury shares) is as follows:
<table_caption>Voting Results for the Amendment of Article (22)</table_caption>
<table>
| Approved | Not Approved | Abstained |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 62.619% | 0% | 21.754% |
</table>

4- The Extraordinary General Assembly approved the amendment of the text of Article (43) of the Articles of Association, as follows:
<table_caption>Comparison of Article (43) Before and After Amendment</table_caption>
<table>
| Text Before Amendment | Text After Amendment |
| :--- | :--- |
| The General Assembly shall convene in an extraordinary session upon a request for a meeting from the Board of Directors or upon a written request addressed to the Board from a number of shareholders holding no less than one-quarter of the company's shares. In this case, the Board of Directors must call for the General Assembly to convene in an extraordinary session within one month from the date of receiving the request. | The Extraordinary General Assembly shall convene upon an invitation from the Board of Directors or upon a reasoned request from shareholders representing fifteen percent of the company's issued capital, or from the Ministry. In this case, the Board of Directors must call for the Extraordinary General Assembly to meet within thirty days from the date of submitting the request. If the Board of Directors does not call for the Assembly within the period |
</table>

The voting result for this item (representing 84.373% of the company's issued capital after excluding treasury shares) is as follows:
<table_caption>Voting Results for the Amendment of Article (43)</table_caption>
<table>
| Approved | Not Approved | Abstained |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 62.619% | 0% | 21.754% |
</table>

5- The Extraordinary General Assembly approved the amendment of Articles (1, 34, 36, 48, 58, 60) of the Articles of Association, as follows:
<table_caption>Amendment to Articles (1, 34, 36, 48, 58, 60) of the Articles of Association</table_caption>
<table>
| Text After Amendment | Text Before Amendment |
| :--- | :--- |
| Amend the phrase: "in accordance with the provisions of Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 25 لسنة 2012</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations" - wherever it appears in the Articles of Association of Kuwait Cement Company - and replace it with the phrase: "in accordance with the provisions of Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations." | Several articles appeared in the Articles of Association, namely Articles (1, 34, 36, 48, 58, 60), all of which refer to and are based on the provisions of Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 25 لسنة 2012</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations. As this latter law has been repealed and is no longer in effect, it requires amendment. |
</table>
The voting result on this item (representing 84.373% of the company's issued share capital after excluding treasury shares) is as follows:
<table_caption>Voting results on the item (representing 84.373% of issued share capital after excluding treasury shares)</table_caption>
<table>
| Abstain | Disagree | Agree |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 21.754% | 0% | 62.619% |
</table>
At the conclusion of the meeting, the Chairman of the Assembly thanked Mr. / Representative of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>, Mr. / Representative of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>, the shareholders, and the attendees, and concluded the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting at 10:50 AM.

Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors

# A'ayan Capital Investment Company <orig>شركة أعيان كابيتال للاستثمار</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
On Sunday, 23/02/2025, the Extraordinary General Assembly of the shareholders of A'ayan Capital Investment Company <orig>شركة أعيان كابيتال للاستثمار</orig> "Under Liquidation" was held at 11:00 AM at the headquarters of A'ayan Leasing and Investment Company <orig>شركة أعيان للإجارة والاستثمار</orig>, located in the Al-Rai <orig>الري</orig> area, Mohammed bin Al-Qasim Street, A'ayan Auto building, first floor.
The meeting was chaired by Mr. / Abdullah Mohammed Al-Shatti <orig>عبد الله محمد الشطي</orig> – the Company Liquidator <orig>مصفي الشركة</orig>.
Also in attendance were: shareholders holding 200,000,000 shares, representing 100% of the company's total share capital.
After announcing that the legal quorum <orig>النصاب القانوني</orig> for convening the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was met, the Chairman opened the meeting by welcoming the attendees. He then proceeded to present the items on the agenda of the Extraordinary General Assembly, and the following took place:
The Ordinary General Assembly of the company reviewed the agenda and took the following resolutions:
Item (1):
Approval was granted to extend the liquidation period for a term of (3) years, commencing from the date of annotation in the Commercial Register.
Item (2):
Approval was granted to reappoint Mr. / Abdullah Mohammed Al-Shatti <orig>عبد الله محمد الشطي</orig> as the company's liquidator.

Chairman of the Board of Directors

# The International Products Company <orig>الشركة الدولية للمنتجات</orig>
## Minutes of the (Adjourned) Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
On Sunday, 23/02/2025, at 12:00 PM, the (adjourned) annual Extraordinary General Assembly meeting of The International Products Company <orig>الشركة الدولية للمنتجات</orig> was held at the headquarters of Kuwait Real Estate Company <orig>شركة عقارات الكويت</orig>, located in the Souk Al-Kuwait building - Block (A) - Eighth Floor - Meeting Room (1), with the attendance of:
1) Mr. / Abdullah Abdulrazzaq Al-Asfour <orig>عبدالله عبدالرزاق العصفور</orig>, Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors – Chairman of the Meeting
Shareholders representing 110,592,839 shares out of the total capital of 154,482,100 shares were present, constituting a percentage of 71.608%.
After the Chairman of the Meeting announced that the legal quorum <orig>النصاب القانوني</orig> for convening the (adjourned) Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was complete, the Assembly began discussing the agenda items, which resulted in the following resolutions:
<table_caption>Amendments to Articles of Association</table_caption>
<table>
| Article After Amendment | Article Before Amendment |
| :--- | :--- |
| **Article (2)** of the Memorandum of Association and Article (1) of the Articles of Association: A Kuwaiti Closed Shareholding Company (K.S.C.C.) <orig>شركة مساهمة كويتية مقفلة (ش.م.ك.م)</orig> named The International Products Company (K.S.C.C.) has been established among the owners of the shares, whose provisions are set out below, in accordance with the provisions of the Companies Law and these Articles of Association. | **Article (2)** of the Memorandum of Association and Article (1) of the Articles of Association: A Kuwaiti Public Shareholding Company (K.P.S.C.) <orig>شركة مساهمة كويتية عامة (ش.م.ك.ع)</orig> named The International Products Company (K.P.S.C.) has been established among the owners of the shares, whose provisions are set out below, in accordance with the provisions of the Companies Law and these Articles of Association. |
| **Article (14)** The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors composed of three members elected by the General Assembly of shareholders by secret ballot. Any shareholder, whether a natural or legal person, may appoint representatives to the company's Board of Directors in proportion to the shares they own. The number of board members selected in this manner shall be deducted from the total number of board members to be elected. Shareholders who have representatives on the Board of Directors may not participate with other shareholders in electing the remaining members of the Board of Directors, except to the extent that exceeds the percentage used to appoint their representative to the Board of Directors. The General Assembly may, upon the request of regulatory authorities, select one or more independent members with experience and competence, provided that their number in this case does not exceed half of the Board members. | **Article (14)** The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors composed of five members elected by the Assembly of shareholders by secret ballot. Any shareholder, whether a natural or legal person, may appoint representatives to the company's Board of Directors in proportion to the shares they own. The number of board members selected in this manner shall be deducted from the total number of board members to be elected. Shareholders who have representatives on the Board of Directors may not participate with other shareholders in electing the remaining members of the Board of Directors, except to the extent that exceeds the percentage used to appoint their representative to the Board of Directors. The General Assembly may, upon the request of regulatory authorities, select one or more independent members with experience and competence, provided that their number in this case does not exceed half of the Board members. |
</table>
After concluding the discussion of the agenda, the Chairman of the Meeting announced the end of the (adjourned) Extraordinary General Assembly meeting at 12:30 PM, and thanked everyone for their attendance and cooperation.

Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors

Board Member via "Webex" video conference
5. Mr. Mazen Essam Hawwa <orig>السيد/ مازن عصام حوا</orig>

Sheikh Abdullah Nasser Al-Sabah <orig>الشيخ عبد الله ناصر الصباح</orig> – Chairman of the Board of Directors – opened the meeting, welcoming the attendees. After the Chairman announced that the legal quorum was met and the meeting was validly convened, the Board began discussing the items on the agenda as follows:

# Agenda of the General Assembly of Burgan Bank:
1. Approval of the Invitation to Shareholders:
Approval of the invitation to the Bank's shareholders for the Sixty-First Annual Ordinary General Assembly meeting at 12:00 PM on Saturday, 05/04/2025, to discuss the agenda (attached).
2. Approval of the Assembly's Agenda:
Approval of the agenda items for the Sixty-First Annual Ordinary General Assembly meeting of Burgan Bank <orig>بنك برقان</orig> shareholders (attached).
3. Approval of Cash Dividend Distribution (6%):
Approval of the Board of Directors' recommendation to distribute cash dividends at a rate of 6% of the nominal value per share (i.e., six fils per share), after deducting treasury shares, to the shareholders registered in the Bank's records at the end of the record date, set for Tuesday, 22/04/2025, to be distributed on Sunday, 27/04/2024. The timeline for share entitlements regarding cash dividends shall be as follows:

<table_caption>Timeline for Cash Dividend Entitlements</table_caption>
<table>
| | |
|:---|:---|
| Share Acquisition Date (Last trading day for the security with entitlements) | Is Thursday, 17/04/2025 |
| Record Date | Is Tuesday, 22/04/2025 |
| First trading day without entitlement (Ex-dividend date) | Is Sunday, 20/04/2025 |
| Cash Dividend Payment Date | Is Sunday, 27/04/2025 |
</table>

4. Approval of Bonus Share Distribution (5%):
Approval of the Board of Directors' proposal to issue 181,240,664 new shares (one hundred eighty-one million, two hundred forty thousand, six hundred sixty-four shares), representing 5% of the issued and paid-up capital, to be distributed as free bonus shares to the shareholders registered in the Bank's records as of the record date, each according to their ownership percentage (at a rate of five shares for every one hundred shares) – in accordance with the Board of Directors' resolution to increase the issued and paid-up capital from KWD 362,481,328/100 (three hundred sixty-two million, four hundred eighty-one thousand, three hundred twenty-eight Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> and one hundred fils) to KWD 380,605,394/500 (three hundred eighty million, six hundred five thousand, three hundred ninety-four Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> and five hundred fils), and to amend Articles (6) of the Memorandum of Association and (5) of the Articles of Association of the Bank accordingly – with this increase, amounting to KWD 18,124,066/400 (eighteen million, one hundred twenty-four thousand, sixty-six Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> and four hundred fils), to be covered from the retained earnings account, and authorizing the Board of Directors to dispose of any resulting fractional shares as it deems appropriate, all subject to obtaining the approvals of the competent authorities. These shares are due to the shareholders registered in the Bank's records at the end of the record date set for Tuesday, 22/04/2024, and will be distributed on 27/04/2024. The timeline for share entitlements regarding the bonus shares shall be as follows:

<table_caption>Timeline for Stock Grant Entitlements</table_caption>
<table>
| | |
|:---|:---|
| Share Acquisition Date (Last trading day for the security with entitlements) | Is Thursday, 17/04/2025 |
| Record Date | Is Tuesday, 22/04/2025 |
| First trading day without entitlement (Ex-dividend date) | Is Sunday, 20/04/2025 |
| The day the bonus shares will be listed in the shareholders' register | Is Sunday, 27/04/2025 |
</table>

5. Authorization:
The Board of Directors has authorized the Chairman of the Board of Directors, the Deputy Chairman of the Board of Directors, the Group Chief Executive Officer, and the Chief Executive Officer – Kuwait, jointly or severally, to make any amendments to the agenda items as they deem necessary to comply with the verbal and written requirements and directives of the regulatory authorities. They are also authorized to set any other date or venue for holding the meeting as they see fit, and to amend the share entitlement schedule, the date of the right to attend the assembly, and the final date for purchasing shares according to any changes to the General Assembly meeting date, and to take all necessary measures to hold the meeting and implement its resolutions.
6. Date of Right to Attend the Ordinary General Assembly and Final Date for Purchasing Shares to Attend the Assembly:
The right to attend the General Assembly will be at the end of the tenth business day preceding the date of the General Assembly, i.e., on 18/03/2024.
The final date for purchasing the company's shares to be registered for the right to attend the General Assembly will be the third business day preceding the right to attend the General Assembly, according to the current settlement cycle, i.e., Thursday, 13/03/2024.
All of the above is without prejudice to any instructions that may be issued by the regulatory authorities in this regard.
7. Approval of the Increase in Issued and Paid-up Capital for the Purpose of Issuing Bonus Shares, and Amending the Article Related to Capital in the Company's Contract Accordingly:
A- Approval of increasing the Bank's issued and paid-up capital from KWD 362,481,328/100 (three hundred sixty-two million, four hundred eighty-one thousand, three hundred twenty-eight Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> and one hundred fils) to KWD 380,605,394/500 (three hundred eighty million, six hundred five thousand, three hundred ninety-four Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> and five hundred fils), by issuing 181,240,664 new shares (one hundred eighty-one million, two hundred forty thousand, six hundred sixty-four shares), representing 5% of the issued capital

# Warba Bank Minutes of the Adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting of Shareholders on Sunday, March 2, 2025

The Adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly of Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig> shareholders was held at 12:30 PM on Sunday, March 2, 2025, at the Bank's head office located in the Sharq <orig>منطقة الشرق</orig> area – Omar Bin Al-Khattab Street <orig>شارع عمر بن الخطاب</orig> – Al-Raya Tower (Administrative) <orig>برج الراية الإداري</orig> – 13th Floor, in the presence of shareholders holding 1,358,498,221 shares, representing 62.214% of the Bank's capital of KWD 218,360,000 (two hundred eighteen million, three hundred sixty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), divided into 2,183,600,000 shares (two billion, one hundred eighty-three million, six hundred thousand shares), distributed as follows:
- Participation via the electronic system by shareholders holding 163,013,740 shares, representing 7.465%.
- Participation through in-person attendance by shareholders holding 1,195,484,481 shares, representing 54.748%.

And in the presence of:
1. Mr. Hamad Musaed Al-Sayer <orig>حمد مساعد الساير</orig>, Chairman of the Board of Directors – Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig>
2. Mr. Shaheen Hamad Al-Ghanem <orig>شاهين حمد الغانم</orig>, Chief Executive Officer – Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig>
3. Mr. Mohammed Musaed Mandi <orig>محمد مساعد مندي</orig>, Director of the Legal Department – Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig>
4. Mr. Mohammed Bouhadi <orig>محمد بوهادي</orig>, Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>

After announcing that the legal quorum for the Adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was met, Mr. Hamad Al-Sayer <orig>حمد الساير</orig> – Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chairman of the General Assembly – opened the meeting by welcoming the attendees. The items on the agenda were then discussed, and the Extraordinary General Assembly passed the following resolutions:
1) Approval was granted to increase the Bank's authorized capital by 100% from KWD 218,360,000 (two hundred eighteen million, three hundred sixty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) divided into 2,183,600,000 shares (two billion, one hundred eighty-three million, six hundred thousand shares) to KWD 436,720,000 (four hundred thirty-six million, seven hundred twenty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) divided into 4,367,200,000 shares (four billion, three hundred sixty-seven million, two hundred thousand shares), and to authorize the General Assembly to delegate to the Board of Directors the authority to call up the issued and paid-up capital within the limits of the authorized capital, with the Board of Directors being authorized to determine the amount and methods of the increase, its call-up dates, and all its terms and conditions, as well as to determine the issue premium for the new shares.
Shareholders holding 4.577% of the capital did not approve this item, without stating reasons.
Shareholders holding 1.193% of the capital abstained from voting, without stating reasons.
2) Approval was granted for the following amendments to the Company's Memorandum of Association <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and/or Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>:
3) To amend Article (7) of the Memorandum of Association <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article (6) of the Company's Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig> as follows:

# Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>

## Announcement
The General Directorate of Nationality and Travel Documents <orig>الإدارة العامة للجنسية ووثائق السفر</orig> announces that the persons whose names are listed below claim to have lost their Kuwaiti passports. Anyone who finds any of them is requested to hand them over to the Directorate within two weeks from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette. Otherwise, these individuals will be issued new Kuwaiti passports in accordance with the established procedures.

### Announcement
The Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> announces the issuance of Practice No. (L.Sh 202/2024 - 2025)
Supply, installation, operation, and maintenance of various machines and equipment and their accessories, and training thereon, for the Technical Stickers Workshop Section <orig>قسم ورشة الملصقات الفنية</orig> – of the General Directorate of Supply and Logistics <orig>الإدارة العامة للإمداد والتموين</orig> (Mechanisms Department <orig>إدارة الآليات</orig>) at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>.
Companies/institutions specialized in this field should contact the General Directorate of Financial Affairs <orig>الإدارة العامة للشئون المالية</orig> – Tenders Department <orig>إدارة المناقصات</orig> (Al-Ardiya Industrial Area <orig>منطقة العارضية الصناعية</orig>) – to obtain the documents for this practice for a fee of (20/-) K.D., only twenty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, non-refundable, via "K-Net". Note that the final insurance for the practice is 10% of the total contract value, and an initial guarantee (to be attached to the financial bid for the practice) must be submitted for each item separately as follows:

<table_caption>Initial Insurance Amounts by Item Number</table_caption>
<table>
| Item No. | Initial Insurance |

Participants must bring a copy of the practice announcement from the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) along with the following documents:
- A valid registration receipt from the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>. or
- A registration request to register with the Ministry and then purchase the practice documents.

Please note that the deadline for submitting bids is Wednesday, 9/4/2025 – at the Bid Opening Committee of the Procurement Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء</orig> at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> building (Sharq Area – Al-Siddiq School <orig>مدرسة الصديق</orig> – First Floor) from 8:00 AM until 1:00 PM. No bids submitted before or after the specified time will be accepted.
A mandatory preliminary meeting will be held with the companies participating in the practice on Thursday, 13/3/2025, at 11:00 AM at the headquarters of the (Mechanisms Department <orig>إدارة الآليات</orig>) of the General Directorate of Supply and Logistics <orig>الإدارة العامة للإمداد والتموين</orig>, to answer companies' inquiries. Note that any recommendations or decisions resulting from this meeting are considered an integral part of the practice documents and are binding on all companies, whether the practitioner attended the mandatory preliminary meeting or not.

</table>

Bids shall be placed in the tender box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
Companies wishing to participate in the tender must meet the following conditions:
1- The local company must be registered in the Supplier Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>.
2- The local company must be specialized in the medical field, documented by a certified certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two separate tender booklets must be purchased with two different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Drug Registration and Control Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية</orig> or proof of certificate submission, and a copy of the manufacturer's and the substance's registration in the Supplier Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, included within the submitted bid contents (specific to Drug Monitoring).
5- Provide samples of new materials, whether it is a new product being requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the relevant monitoring authority (Medicines – Medical Supplies).
6- Attach a National Labor Support percentage certificate.
7- Tender documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
8- The fees for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the tender documents.
9- Price quotations must be submitted in a sealed envelope, inclusive of the tender documents, by the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.# Announcement

Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee
No. 2025/06 held on 2025/02/16

After reviewing the applications submitted for the amendment of data in the births and deaths records, it was decided to list the amendment below in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>). If the committee does not receive any objection within fifteen days from the date of publication of this announcement, the amendment will be made in the records, and birth or death certificates will be issued in accordance with the following amendment:

Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee
No. 2025/06 held on 2025/02/16

The Births and Deaths Committee, stipulated in Article 15 of Law No. 36/69 and formed by Ministerial Resolution No. 1650/2021, convened.
Mr. / Director of the Central Registry for Births and Deaths, Chairman
Dr. / Head of the General Medical Council, Member
Ms. / Head of the Research and Opinion Department, Member
Mr. / Head of the Registration Department, Member
Mr. / Head of the Deaths Department, Member
Mr. / Legal Researcher, Member
Mr. / Head of the Records Department, Member
The secretarial duties of the committee were performed by Ms. Alia Al-Saffar <orig>علياء الصفار</orig>.

The committee reviewed applications from No. ((77)) to No. ((88)) in the attached list concerning the amendment of data in the births and deaths records for requests of unrecorded births and deaths. After examination and verification of the completeness of documents and records, the committee decides to announce the amendments and requests in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) in two consecutive issues. If the legal period (fifteen days) from the date of the last announcement elapses without any objection being submitted, the amendments will be made in the registers, and birth and death certificates will be issued.

Director of the Central Registry for Births
Head of the Records Department
Committee Secretary
Head of the Research and Opinion Department
Head of the Registration Department
Head of the Deaths Department
Legal Researcher
Head of the General Medical Council
