<header>
26
Kuwait Today Issue 1729, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 9 Ramadan 1446 H - 9/3/2025 G
</header>
** And according to the expert's report:
The disputed property is located in the Abdullah Al-Mubarak area, Block (3), Street No. (302), House No. (35), Plot No. (391), and was inspected as follows:
- The disputed property is a private residence overlooking three streets and consists of a basement, ground floor, first floor, and second floor. The facade is yellow mosaic. It has (5) entrances, central air conditioning, and contains an elevator.
- The first entrance leads to a diwaniya.
- The second entrance leads to an office.
- The third entrance leads to a hallway and a staircase leading to the first and second floors, and an elevator leading to the basement, first, and second floors.
- The fourth entrance leads to an entryway leading to a hall on the ground floor and an external staircase leading to the basement.
- The fifth entrance leads to a kitchen on the ground floor.
- The basement consists of (3 rooms + bathroom + hall + swimming pool + shower room + master bedroom with bathroom + driver's room with bathroom + courtyard).
- The ground floor consists of (office + 3 bathrooms + diwaniya + hall + kitchen + storage room).
- There are newly installed plasterboard partitions on the ground floor between the hall and the diwaniya, between the office and the staircase leading to the basement, and between the hallway containing the elevator and the hall.
- The first floor consists of (5) master bedrooms with bathrooms + a hall).
- The second floor consists of (a laundry room + a master bedroom with a bathroom + two apartments).
- 1- The first apartment consists of (a hall + a master bedroom with a bathroom + a kitchen + a storage room + a laundry room + 2 rooms + a bathroom).
- 2- The second apartment consists of (a hall + 2 rooms + a kitchen with a room + a bathroom).
- The roof contains an equipment room.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
1.  **First:** The auction begins at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Directorate at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
2.  **Second:** The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
3.  **Third:** If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
4.  **Fourth:** If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
5.  **Fifth:** If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at their liability on the basis of the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
6.  **Sixth:** The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
7.  **Seventh:** This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
8.  **Eighth:** The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Notice:
1.  This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2.  The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3.  The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease agreement in their favor for a comparable rent."

President of the Court of First Instance

# Announcement of the Public Auction Sale of Two Properties
The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction sale of the two properties described below on Monday, 7/4/2025, in Hall 48 on the second floor of the Justice Palace at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 361/2024 Sales/1.

**Filed by:**
The Director General of the Public Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig>, in his capacity, legally represented by the Fatwa and Legislation Department <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig>.

**Against:**
**First:** The heirs of the late Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>, the heirs of the late Raj'a Mohammed Shanoon Marzouq <orig>رجعه محمد شنون مرزوق</orig>, the heirs of the late Ahmed Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>أحمد محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>, and the heirs of the late Fuhaid Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>فهيد محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig> (full siblings), who are:
1.  Nafi' Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>نافع محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.
2.  Lafi Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>لافي محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.
3.  Doukhi Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>دوخي محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.
4.  Abdullah Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>عبدالله محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.
5.  Nawaf Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>نواف محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.
6.  Manayer Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>مناير محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.
7.  Jamila Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>جميله محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.
8.  Sheikha Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>شيخة محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.
9.  Moudhi Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>موضي محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>.

**Second:** The heirs of the late Fuhaid Mohammed Hisyan Al-Fuhaid <orig>فهيد محمد حصيان الفهيد</orig>, the maternal half-siblings, who are:
1.  Fahad bin Mulhim bin Ali Al-Saqri Al-Anzi <orig>فهد بن ملحم بن علي الصقري العنزي</orig>.

  "page_summary": "This page contains two legal announcements from the Plenary Court regarding public property auctions, detailing the properties, involved parties, auction dates, base prices, and conditions."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1729 Seventy-First Year
27
Sunday, 9 Ramadan 1446 H - 9/3/2025 G
</header>


2- Duha Hasban Mohammed Al-Fahad <orig>ضحى حسبان محمد الفهيد</orig>.
3- Anwar Hasban Mohammed Al-Fahad <orig>أنوار حسبان محمد الفهيد</orig>.
Fourth: The Assistant Undersecretary for Real Estate Registration and Notarization Affairs at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>, in his capacity.

## Description of the First Property: (According to the attached description certificate)
1- Property of Document No. 2020/8241 located in the Al-Funaitis <orig>الفنيطيس</orig> area - Plot (46), Block No. (2), Plan M/37882 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold at public auction with a starting price of KWD 480,000 (Four hundred and eighty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** And according to the description certificate:
- Vacant land.
** And according to the expert's report:
Plot No. 46 corresponds to Document No. 2020/8241, is located on two streets at a corner location, is bordered by one neighbor, and is a vacant plot of land.

## Description of the Second Property: (According to the attached description certificate)
2- Property of Document No. 2020/8241 located in the Al-Funaitis <orig>الفنيطيس</orig> area - Plot (48), Block No. (2), Plan M/37882 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold at public auction with a starting price of KWD 380,000 (Three hundred and eighty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** And according to the description certificate:
- Vacant land.
** And according to the expert's report:
Plot No. 48 corresponds to Document No. 2020/8241, is located on one street, is adjacent to Plot 46, and is a vacant plot of land.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the starting price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is accepted by the judge must deposit the full accepted price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was accepted does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding will be immediately reopened at their liability based on the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures, without any liability on the part of the Clerk's Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig>.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment <orig>حكم رسو المزاد</orig> is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease agreement in their favor for a comparable rent."

President of the Court of First Instance

---

**And according to the expert's report:
The property subject of the dispute, located in the Al-Riggae <orig>الرقاب</orig> area, Block <orig>قطعة</orig> 2, Street 2, Plot <orig>قسيمة</orig> 383, House 19, Automated Address Number: 13229488, where the expert found the following after inspection and examination:
The property subject of the dispute conforms in location and area to the ownership document, sale contract No. 17897, issued by the Department of Real Estate Registration and Documentation <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig> on 21/12/1997, with an area of 400 m2.
The property is an old, private residence with an exterior cladding of white Jordanian stone. The house is located on two streets (front and back) and a side alley, with a neighbor on one side only. Its main facade has a setback used as a parking area shaded by a Kirby structure, with a traffic island opposite it. The rear facade has a large, paved setback overlooking a main street.
The property consists of a ground floor, a first floor, and a roof, as detailed below:
The ground floor consists of (3 reception halls + a diwaniya with a bathroom + a maid's room + a driver's room with a bathroom + a main kitchen + a washroom with a toilet + a bathroom).
The first floor consists of (a living hall + 2 master bedrooms with bathrooms + 3 bedrooms + a kitchenette + a bathroom).
The property generally has a standard level of finishing, with central air conditioning and ceramic flooring.
The expert found that the property subject of the dispute is used as a family residence. The first defendant, among her children, stated that she occupies the property with her children, the first-named defendants, except for the sixth.
The appointed expert from the administration reviewed the property document, inspected the property, and took the necessary notes in preparation for estimating its value.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session offering to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction will be reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction shall be immediately reopened at their liability based on the price at which it was previously awarded to them. In this session, no bid will be considered unless accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures. The Clerk's Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bears no responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session offering to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price

Against: Yaqoub Haji Hussein Karashi <orig>يعقوب حاجي حسين كراشي</orig>.
-Property Description (according to the attached description certificate)
The property of Document No. 8902/1996, located in the Mubarak Al-Kabeer <orig>مبارك الكبير</orig> area - Plot No. 3 - Parcel 93 - Plan M/37041 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold at public auction with a starting price of KWD 346,500 (Three hundred forty-six thousand five hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
**- According to the description certificate, the following violations exist:
1- An additional structure made of light materials on the roof.
2- There is a room on the roof of the ground floor.
** And according to the expert's report
In the session of 17/11/2023, the plaintiff's representative stated that she requests the expertise of valuation experts <orig>خبراء الدراية</orig> to assess the value of the disputed property due to the parties' failure to agree on sorting and partitioning <orig>فرز والتجنيب</orig>. When asked about the valuation of the consideration for use mentioned in the statement of claim, she stated that she only requests the experts to sort and partition the property as stated in the assignment. She submitted a portfolio of documents including a copy of a document (sale contract) No. (8902) dated 05/08/1996, according to which the property located in the Al-Qurain area, parcel No. (93) of plan No. (M/37041), sector (H), with an area of (400 m²), is described as a private residence owned jointly and equally by / Yaqoub Haji Hussein Karashi <orig>يعقوب حاجي حسين كراشي</orig> (the defendant) and Samira Mousa Mohammed Al-Gharib <orig>سميرة موسى محمد الغريب</orig> (the plaintiff).
2) In the session of 26/01/2023, we proceeded to the Mubarak Al-Kabeer <orig>مبارك الكبير</orig> area, Plot (3), Street (5), House (18), Parcel (93), where the disputed property is located, accompanied by the valuation expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig>, Mr. / Faisal Al-Sharhan <orig>فيصل الشرهان</orig>. Both parties failed to attend. The inspection was carried out as follows:
- The disputed property is a private residence located on two internal secondary streets. One street is separated from the property by a setback used as a garden and parking. There is also a pedestrian side alley, and the other side is adjacent to a neighbor. It consists of (basement, ground floor, first floor, second floor, roof). The building condition is good, it has central air conditioning, and there is an elevator.
- During the inspection, upon knocking on the door, Mr. / Hassan Yaqoub Haji Karashi <orig>حسن يعقوب حاجي كراشي</orig> allowed the experts to enter and inspect the disputed property, stating that he is the son of the defendant.
- Basement floor: Consists of (two halls, a bathroom with washbasins).
- Ground floor: Consists of (two halls, two rooms, a kitchen, a bathroom).
- First floor: Consists of (a hall, 5 rooms, 3 bathrooms, a preparatory kitchen).
- Second floor: Consists of (a hall, 4 rooms, 4 bathrooms, a preparatory kitchen, a laundry room).
- Roof floor: Consists of (a room, a bathroom, a storage room).
- The valuation expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> inspected the property on-site in preparation for his report on the value of the disputed property.
3) On 31/01/2023, we received the valuation expert's <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> report on the value of the disputed property, which was estimated at an amount of (KWD 385,000).

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction begins at the starting price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at their liability based on the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. Those initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease contract in their favor for a comparable rent."
President of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

6- Tariq Abdulghaffar Haidar Ma'rafi <orig>طارق عبدالغفار حيدر معرفي</orig>.
- Property Description (according to the attached description certificate)
The property of Document No. 4531/1992, located in the Al-Jabriya <orig>الجابرية</orig> area – Plot No. 5 – Parcel 3 – Plan M/33925 – with an area of 1080 m², to be sold at public auction with a starting price of KWD 963,000 (Nine hundred sixty-three thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the description certificate, there is a violation:
The installation of an elevator.
** According to the expert's report
- The disputed property is located in the Al-Jabriya <orig>الجابرية</orig> area, Plot 5, Street 104, Parcel 108, House 42, with the automated address number 90509723.
- The disputed property is a parcel with an area of 1080 square meters, fronting two streets (front and back), one street near the roundabout and a back street overlooking an unpaved square, with entrances from both said sides.
- The expert found that the disputed property consists of a ground floor, a first floor, and a roof, with buildings in the side yard of the disputed property, and with setbacks at the front and back.
- The disputed property is clad on the exterior with a somewhat old reddish-yellow stone. There is a garden in the house's courtyard and a separate building belonging to the defendant, Amal Abdulghaffar Haidar <orig>آمال عبد الغفار حيدر</orig>, which consists of a room with a unit air conditioner, a living room, and a bathroom.
- The expert found a separate Diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> building in the house's courtyard. The defendants' attending agent stated that it is used by the plaintiffs for smoking, measures 7m x 5m, has unit air conditioning, and has new finishes.
- The expert moved to the house and found it has two entrances, a side entrance by the kitchen. It was found that the ground floor consists of a first living room, a second living room, an internal kitchen, and a bathroom. The attending agent stated that these are also used independently by all parties to the lawsuit, including the plaintiffs.
- The expert found a room and a bathroom for the defendant, Nidhal Abdulghaffar Haidar <orig>نضال عبد الغفار حيدر</orig>. It was also found that there is one staircase in the middle of the living room, an elevator, central air conditioning, and the floors are beige marble.
- The expert proceeded to the first floor and found a furnished and equipped empty room, which the agent stated is used by the plaintiffs whenever any of them wish to be present.
- The expert found a living room and two rooms between them on the first floor, and the attending agent stated that they are sometimes used by the plaintiffs. There are also two rooms with a bathroom between them, which the agent stated are used independently by the defendant, Tariq Abdulghaffar Haidar <orig>طارق عبد الغفار حيدر</orig>.
- At 11:18, the third defendant, Manal Abdulghaffar Ma'rafi <orig>منال عبد الغفار معرفي</orig>, arrived and requested to have her presence recorded and to confirm the attending agent's statement regarding the occupants of the property.
- The expert proceeded to the roof of the property and found two central air conditioning units and a red tile roof. The expert found that the courtyard of the disputed property has tiled flooring, and there are plants, palm trees, and unused setbacks.
- The technical expert took his notes in preparation for drafting the report on the property's value and the quarterly rental value of the disputed property.
- The expert asked the third defendant, Manal Abdulghaffar Ma'rafi <orig>منال عبد الغفار معرفي</orig>, about the number of current occupants of the disputed property. She stated that they are (Nidhal, Amal, and Tariq) Abdulghaffar Ma'rafi <orig>(نضال وآمال وطارق) عبد الغفار معرفي</orig>, in addition to the plaintiffs entering and using the disputed property whenever they wish, and that they have two external keys. She stated that they enter the property's living room and are not prohibited from entering the property.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the starting price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Directorate at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is accepted by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full accepted price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was accepted does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction award will be ruled in their favor, unless someone comes forward in that session who is willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding is immediately reopened at their liability on the basis of the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. Those initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to execute a lease agreement in their favor for a comparable rent."
President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

Second: Heirs of the late Ali Nouri Hassan Issa <orig>علي نوري حسن عيسى</orig>:
1- Abdulaziz Ali Nouri Hassan Issa <orig>عبدالعزيز علي نوري حسن عيسى</orig>.

Description of the First Property: (According to the attached Description Certificate)
The property of Document No. 2009/2923 located in the Al-Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig> area – Plot (800) Block No. (1) Plan M/32097 – with an area of 257 m2, to be sold by public auction with a base price of KWD 260,000, two hundred and sixty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.
**According to the Description Certificate:
There is an unpermitted construction within the property boundaries on the ground floor with a total area of 17m2, an unpermitted construction outside the property boundaries with an area of 6m2, on the first floor an unpermitted construction with an area of 11m2 within the property boundaries, and an unpermitted construction outside the property boundaries with an area of 6m2. On the second floor, an unpermitted Kirby building with an area of 18m2 was constructed.
**According to the Expert's Report:
The property subject of the lawsuit, in execution of the referral judgment, is located in the Al-Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig> area – Block 1 – Avenue 4 – Plot No. 800, and bears the Automated Number (14000749). The inspection was conducted as follows:
The disputed property is a private residence in an old construction condition, located on two streets (front and back), a main internal street (Avenue 4) and an internal street, and is bordered by two neighbors on the sides.
The property consists of a ground floor and a first floor, and a Kirby room has been added on the roof, clad with stone, and the property has window air conditioning.
The second plaintiff guided the expert on the components of the disputed property and stated that the property consists of two buildings, as follows:
The first building has one entrance leading to the internal street, and it consists of:
- Ground floor: Hall - kitchen - bedroom - bathroom.
- First floor: Three (3) bedrooms - bathroom - hall.
- Roof: A separate Kirby room used as a storage room.
The second plaintiff and the fifteenth defendant, Mr. Abdullah Nouri Hassan Issa <orig>عبد الله نوري حسن عيسى</orig>, stated that this part is occupied by the fifteenth defendant and his mother, Mrs. Felicisima Nouri Hassan Issa <orig>فيليسيسيما نوري حسن عيسى</orig> (the sixth defendant).
There is a corridor in the yard that separates the two buildings, and in the kitchen of the first building on the ground floor, there is a door leading to this corridor.
The other building has two entrances overlooking the main internal street (Avenue 4) and has a setback in front of it. It consists of:
- Ground floor: Hall - kitchen - three (3) bedrooms - bathroom. There are stairs leading to the first floor of this building, but they have been closed off. The second plaintiff and the fifteenth defendant stated that this part is neglected and not occupied by any of the heirs. First floor: The second plaintiff and the fifteenth defendant stated that this part of the property is occupied by the sixteenth defendant, Najat Owais Abu Al-Ela <orig>نجاة عويس أبو العلا</orig>, and that she is not currently present in the house. They provided the expert with the components of this part, which consists of two (2) halls - two bedrooms - a kitchen - a bathroom.
The appointed expert took all his notes in preparation for estimating the value of the land and the buildings thereon.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice.
Second: Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, as well as the expenses and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding shall be reopened at his liability during the same session, based on the price at which the sale had been awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction award shall be judged in his favor, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with an increase of one-tenth, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the one-tenth increase, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at his liability based on the price that had been awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid shall be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the expenses of the execution procedures amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. The parties initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, and the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> shall bear no liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date the judgment is pronounced, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease contract in his favor for a rent equivalent to the market rate."

President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

Filed by:
Hamoud Fahad Jassem Al-Dabbous <orig>حمود فهد جاسم الدبوس</orig>.

Sunday, 9 Ramadan 1446 AH - 09/03/2025 AD

Against:
1- Talal Fahad Jassem Al-Dabbous <orig>طلال فهد جاسم الدبوس</orig>, in his personal capacity and as the legal representative of Al-Alamia for Cargo Transport Company <orig>شركة العالمية لنقل البضائع</orig>.
2- Abdulaziz Mohammed Abdulaziz Al-Banwan <orig>عبدالعزيز محمد عبدالعزيز البنوان</orig> – Intervening party.

Description of the Share in the Property: (According to the attached Certificate of Description)
An undivided share of 50% of the property under Document No. 2008/5199, located in the Al-Fahaheel <orig>الفحيحيل</orig> area – Plot (8), Parcel No. (33), Plan M/24516 – with a total area of 732 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 600,000 (six hundred thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) for the share offered for sale.

** And according to the Certificate of Description:
- Existence of a violation: 1- A violation on the first ground floor by increasing the area of the annexes by 30 m². 2- A violation on the ground floor by building an apartment with an area of 45 m². 3- A violation on the services floor by building two apartments with an area of 120 m².

** And according to the Expert's Report:
The disputed property located in the Al-Fahaheel <orig>الفحيحيل</orig> area, Block 8, Street 27, Plot 3308, Building 6, PACI No. 93268646, was inspected as follows:
1. The property subject of the lawsuit is located on a single street, bordered by neighbors on three sides, and has a small, paved, unshaded setback at the front, used as parking.
2. The property subject of the lawsuit is an old-finish investment residential building, with its exterior clad in beige-colored Sigma paint, and an area of 732 square meters, pursuant to title deed of sale contract No. 5199 dated 24/03/2008.
3. The property subject of the lawsuit is a building consisting of a ground floor and 11 repeated floors, with the following details:
- The ground floor consists of 11 small annexes, where 4 of them consist of two rooms, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchenette, and 7 of them consist of one room, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchenette.
- The repeated floors (11 floors) each consist of 4 apartments, and each apartment consists of two rooms, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchen.
- The disputed property has an old-level finish. The finishes on the ground floor and in the corridors have ceramic flooring, split-unit air conditioning, standard suspended lighting, gypsum decorations, and plain painted walls.
5. The expert inspected one of the apartments, which has ceramic flooring, a central air conditioning system, standard suspended lighting, gypsum ceiling decorations, and plain painted walls. The building's janitor stated that all apartments are identical to this one. The expert also inspected one of the annexes, which has the same finish as the apartments, except for the split-unit air conditioning.

Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at his liability in the same session based on the price at which the sale had been awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction award will be adjudged to him, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at his liability on the basis of the price that had been awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, lawyer's and expert's fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to issue a lease contract in his favor for a fair market rent."

President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

---

**Against:**
1- Raha Marzouq Abdullah Al-Maran <orig>راحه مرزوق عبدالله المران</orig>.
2- Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice for Real Estate Registration and Notarization Affairs <orig>وكيل وزارة العدل لشئون التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig>, in his capacity.

**First: Description of the property according to the attached description certificate:**
The property of Document No. 5021 dated 5/5/2019, located in the Zahra Suburb <orig>ضاحية الزهراء</orig> area, Block 6, Plot 277 of Plan No. 32903, with an area of 400 m², to be sold by public auction with a base price of (640,000 K.D.) six hundred and forty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.

It consists of a ground floor, first floor, second floor, and a rooftop, with an area of 456 m² according to the document, and has two entrances.
The property conforms to Document No. 14342/1998 in terms of area and general and specific specifications.
The door was knocked on and opened by the second defendant, who stated that the ground floor consists of: a hall + a master bedroom with an attached bathroom + two rooms + a bathroom + a kitchen + a diwaniya with an attached bathroom + a driver's room with an attached bathroom. It is leased to a third party for an amount of 700 K.D., and the expert was unable to inspect it.
The first floor consists of a hall + a kitchen + 6 rooms + 3 bathrooms, and it is occupied by the second defendant and her children.
The second floor consists of a hall + a kitchen + 6 rooms + 3 bathrooms, and it is occupied by the second defendant's brother, according to the second defendant's statement, as the expert was unable to inspect it.
Rooftop: a laundry room + a maid's room + two rooms + a kitchen + a bathroom + a hall. According to the second defendant's statement, the rooftop is leased to a third party in exchange for repairing the air conditioning for the entire property in case of malfunction, and the expert was unable to inspect it.

**Attachments:**
1- Raha Marzouq Abdullah Al-Maran <orig>راحه مرزوق عبدالله المران</orig>.
2- Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice for Real Estate Registration and Notarization Affairs <orig>كيل وزارة العدل لشئون التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig>, in his capacity.
First: Description of the property according to the attached description certificate.
The property of Document No. 5021 dated 5/5/2019, located in the Zahra Suburb <orig>ضاحية الزهراء</orig> area, Block 6, Plot 277 of Plan No. 32903, with an area of 400 m², to be sold by public auction with a base price of (640,000 K.D.) six hundred and forty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.

** And according to the expert's report dated 19/5/2024, the disputed house was visited and inspected as follows:
The subject of the dispute is located in the Al-Zahra <orig>الزهراء</orig> area – Block 6 – Street 44 – House 41. It is a private residence consisting of a ground, first, and second floor. The facade is stone, the building condition is new, and it overlooks a main street. The property is fully leased, which made it impossible to inspect from the inside. Its area is 400 m².

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall start at the base price indicated for the property. To participate in the auction, a payment of at least one-fifth of that price is required by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at their liability on the basis of the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request of those initiating the sale procedures and at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease contract in their favor for a similar rent."

President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

The second plaintiff stated that one of the apartments is occupied by his son, and the other apartment is locked, unoccupied, and in the possession of the first defendant.
- The rooftop consists of 2 rooms + a bathroom, and the floor is unoccupied.
- The property has central air conditioning and an elevator.
- The expert found that the property does not generate income and is not leased.

## Announcement of a Criminal Judgment
The Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>, in its session held on 23-02-2021, issued a judgment in Case No. 20/005477 - Court of First Instance, Ordinary Misdemeanors
Police Station No.: (19/0000735 - Special Misdemeanors)
Automated Case No.: 202374510
Against the defendant: Ilagiya Samy Ilagobo Ilagobo <orig>ايلاغيا سامي ايلاغوبو ايلاغوبو</orig>
Nationality: India, Civil ID No.: 284041809292
An in-absentia judgment was issued, ruling:
To fine the defendant two hundred dinars for the charge brought against him.
The Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig> hereby notifies the convicted person of this judgment and directs all security authorities to enforce it in accordance with the text of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedure and Trials. It is noted that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the day following publication, elapses without the convicted person challenging the judgment through opposition or appeal, the judgment shall become final and enforceable against him.
Director of the Criminal Enforcement Prosecution <orig>مدير نيابة التنفيذ الجنائي</orig>

It should be noted that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the day following publication, elapses without the convicted person challenging the judgment through opposition or appeal, the judgment becomes final and enforceable against him.
Director of the Criminal Enforcement Prosecution

# Announcement
The following is a necessary correction to the material error that occurred in the announcement of the "Annual Plan of the Ministry of Electricity, Water, and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> for the Fiscal Year (2020-2021)," published in the Official Gazette "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>" Issue No. (1492) dated 19/07/2020.

<table_caption>Correction to the Annual Plan for the Ministry of Electricity, Water, and Renewable Energy (2020-2021)</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Material Error | Correction |
|---|---|---|
| 1 | A material error occurred in Eighthly – Item No. (19), where the project name was stated as follows: << Supply and extension of 132 kV underground cables to supply various areas in Al-Ahmadi Governorate <orig>محافظة الأحمدي</orig> | The correct version is: << Design, supply, and extension of 132 kV underground cables to supply various areas in Al-Ahmadi Governorate <orig>محافظة الأحمدي</orig> and to reinforce the 132 kV and 33 kV electrical grid in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> >> |
</table>

The following is a necessary addition to the announcement of the "Annual Plan of the Ministry of Electricity and Water for the Fiscal Year (2024-2025)," published in the Official Gazette "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>" Issue No. (1685) dated 05/05/2024.

 according to the following data:

1- Location for receiving the terms and conditions booklet and submitting bids for the two auctions: Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> – General Directorate of Supply <orig>الإدارة العامة للإمداد</orig> "Vehicles Department <orig>إدارة الآليات</orig>" – Subhan, from March 9, 2025, to March 13, 2025. The documents will be handed over for a fee of (100) Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> to be paid to the Ministry of Interior's treasury, noting that two separate documents will be sold:
a- Auction No. (2453): Document for the sale of (80) vehicles (Group Two): 76 partial write-offs and 4 total write-offs.
b- Auction No. (2454): Document for the sale of (80) vehicles (Group Three): 72 partial write-offs and 8 total write-offs.
Upon receiving the terms and conditions booklet, the bidder will sign a declaration and pledge to adhere to the specified date for submitting the bid to the Central Sales Committee <orig>لجنة البيع المركزي</orig> at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.
2- Inspection Date: (5) working days from March 9, 2025 – March 13, 2025
Inspection Time: During official working hours.
3- Location for receiving bidders wishing to inspect:
Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> – Mina Abdullah Scrap Yard.
4- Date for submitting bids and opening envelopes:
- Bids are to be submitted on Monday, March 17, 2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> – Block 12 – Third Floor – General Warehousing Affairs Department <orig>إدارة شؤون التخزين العامة</orig> – Central Sales Section <orig>قسم البيع المركزي</orig>, according to the time specified for the bidder by the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> (No bid will be accepted after the bidder's specified time has passed).
- Envelopes will be opened and the auction held on Tuesday, March 18, 2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> – Block 12 – Third Floor – General Warehousing Affairs Department <orig>إدارة شؤون التخزين العامة</orig>.
- The winning bidder will be announced on the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> website on Tuesday, March 18, 2025.
- Checks will be returned to unsuccessful bidders on Wednesday, March 19, 2025.
- Certified checks / bank guarantees must be made out in the name of the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>.
- Special conditions for bidders:
1. The bidder must be a Kuwaiti citizen – individual or company – registered in the Commercial Register and with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>. A foreigner may participate provided they have a Kuwaiti partner or agent who is a merchant under a notarized contract. (Must attach: a copy of the Chamber of Commerce and Industry certificate, a copy of the company license, a copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig>, and an authorization letter certified by the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, all of which must be valid).
2. Kuwaiti individuals are allowed to participate in the auction (a copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig> must be attached).
3. The winning bidder for the scrap car auction must, at their own expense, completely remove the primary color of the vehicles at their location before they are removed or their ownership is transferred, under the supervision of specialists from the Ministry's Vehicles Department <orig>إدارة الآليات</orig>.
4. The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> is not responsible for transferring the vehicles to the winning bidder's name at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>.
- To receive the terms and conditions booklet, bidders may contact: Major / Fahad Abdullah Al-Ajmi <orig>فهد عبدالله العجمي</orig>, Phone: 60662667,
First Lieutenant Engineer / Ahmed Mahmoud Al-Tamimi <orig>احمد محمود التميمي</orig>, Phone: 66969658, First Lieutenant Engineer / Mohammed Walid Al-Abdulsalam <orig>محمد وليد العبدالسلام</orig>, Phone: 98885857.
- Inspection site official for bidders: First Lieutenant Engineer / Ahmed Mahmoud Al-Tamimi <orig>احمد محمود التميمي</orig>

# Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig>
## Announcement
The Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig> announces the publication of the announcement for the re-tendering of Practice No. H.A./Sh.A.M./55 - 2024/2025 regarding the provision of equipment for the Deanship of Library Affairs and the provision of a security gate (Central Library), in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents.
Companies and institutions wishing to participate in this practice should visit the website of the Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig> (www.Paet.edu.kw) to purchase the tender documents for the practice, listed under electronic services (general services), for a non-refundable fee of (75/- K.D.). Bids are to be submitted to the Authority's main office located in the Shuwaikh Educational Area – Procurement Department within one week from this date.
Director General <orig>المدير العام</orig>

## Announcement
The Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig> announces the publication of the announcement for Practice No. 96-2024/2025 regarding the graduation ceremony for students of the Public Authority for Applied Education and Training, in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents.
Companies and institutions wishing to participate in this practice should visit the website of the Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig> (www.Paet.edu.Kw) to purchase the tender documents for the practice, listed under electronic services (general services). Bids are to be submitted to the Authority's main office located in the Shuwaikh Educational Area – Procurement Department within one week from this date for a non-refundable fee of (75.000 K.D.).
Director General <orig>المدير العام</orig>

# Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>
## Announcement
The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces that Messrs./ Jassim Hassan Ali Rubaithel <orig>جاسم حسن علي ربيثل</orig> have applied for a replacement for a lost license, License No.: (30075), issued on: 16-12-2006, under the trade name: Kuwaiti Architects Group Factory for Wooden Carpentry Works, designated for: Wooden Carpentry Works.
Location
Area: West Shuaiba Industrial Area. Owner's Name: Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>
Plot: 5, Parcel: B125-B126, Shop: Floor: Building: -
Anyone who has the aforementioned license in their possession or has any information regarding it is requested to come forward to the headquarters of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>, ground floor, within two weeks from the date of this announcement's publication. Otherwise, after the expiration of this period, the Authority will issue a replacement for the requested lost license.

# Public Authority for Civil Information <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig>
## Announcement
The Public Authority for Civil Information <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig> announces that the individuals listed below have had their residential addresses canceled in its records (based on a declaration by the property owner or the demolition of the building). These individuals must report to the Authority to register their new address (after providing supporting documents) within thirty days from this date. Failure to do so will result in the penalty stipulated in Article (33) of Law No. 32 of 1982, which is a fine not exceeding one hundred dinars, multiplied by the number of persons.

# Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>
## Announcement
### Award of Practice No. (15-2024/2025)
Regarding the supply, development, and maintenance of the electronic signature for the Central Agency for Information Technology
The Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig> announces the award of Practice No. (15-2024/2025) regarding the supply, development, and maintenance of the electronic signature for the Central Agency for Information Technology to Al-Diyar United Company for Trading and Contracting <orig>شركة الديار المتحدة للتجارة والمقاولات</orig>.

# Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>
## Minutes of Meeting No. (2025/18)
**Held on the morning of (Monday)**
**03 Ramadan 1446 H, corresponding to 03-03-2025 G**

The Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> held its session No. (2025/18) at ten o'clock on the morning of (Monday), 03-03-2025, with the attendance of the following gentlemen:

<table_caption>Board Members of the Central Agency for Public Tenders</table_caption>
<table>
| | | |
|:---:|:---|:---|
| 1 | Mr. Essam Daoud Al-Marzouq <orig>عصام داود المرزوق</orig> | Chairman of the Central Agency for Public Tenders |
| 2 | Mrs. Haifa Fahad Al-Jarallah <orig>هيفاء فهد الجار الله</orig> | Vice Chairman of the Central Agency for Public Tenders |
| 3 | Mr. Abdullah Mohammed Theyab <orig>عبد الله محمد ذياب</orig> | Member of the Central Agency for Public Tenders |
| 4 | Dr. Abdullah Ahmed Al-Khayat <orig>عبد الله أحمد الخياط</orig> | Member of the Central Agency for Public Tenders |
| 5 | Eng. Ahmed Ali Qasem <orig>أحمد علي قاسم</orig> | Member of the Central Agency for Public Tenders |
| 6 | Mr. Osama Khaled Boodai <orig>أسامة خالد بودي</orig> | Member of the Central Agency for Public Tenders |
| 7 | Mrs. Taiba Yousef Al-Qaindi <orig>طيبة يوسف القيندي</orig> | Member of the Central Agency for Public Tenders |
| 8 | Dr. Fahad Farhan Tarman Al-Azmi <orig>فهد فرحان طرمان العازمي</orig> | Member / Representative of the Fatwa and Legislation Department |
| 9 | Mr. Khaled Al-Kandari <orig>خالد الكندري</orig> | Member Representative / Ministry of Finance |
| 10 | Dr. Abdullah Salem Al-Rashidi <orig>عبدالله سالم الرشيدي</orig> | Member / Representative of the Public Authority for Manpower |
| 11 | Mr. Abdullah Al-Sarraf <orig>عبدالله الصراف</orig> | Member / Representative of the General Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Planning and Development |
| 12 | Dr. Barjas Al-Dosari <orig>برجس الدوسري</orig> | Member / Representative of the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development |
</table>

**Secretary-General:**
<table_caption>General Secretary of the Central Agency for Public Tenders</table_caption>
<table>
| | | |
|:---:|:---|:---|
| 1 | Mr. Anwar Ahmed Al-Dhahiri <orig>أنور أحمد الظواهري</orig> | Secretary-General of the Central Agency for Public Tenders |
</table>

These minutes were signed and approved by the Chairman and members of the Agency's Board on 03-03-2025, in accordance with Article (8) of the Executive Regulations.

Also in attendance for part of the meeting were the members/representatives of government entities, as follows:

## Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>
### Bid Opening
<table_caption>Tender Decision No. 1 for the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Statement | Subject |
|:---:|:---|:---|
| 1 | Number: - MEW / 28/2023/2024 | Tender for maintenance works for the Doha Reverse Osmosis Seawater Desalination Plant with equipment for increasing the alkalinity of produced water (Phase One). Decision No. (1) of Meeting No. (2025/18). The bids submitted for the tender, numbering (5), were opened as recorded in the price schedule. The Agency's Board of Directors decided to refer the submitted bid documents to the concerned entity for study and to provide the necessary recommendations thereon within (30) days from this date. |
| 2 | Number: - MEW / 44/2023/2024 | Tender for the management and maintenance of the smart meter system (systems, programs, and devices) and its associated communications network for the main and alternative sites of the Customer Services Sector. Decision No. (2) of Meeting No. (2025/18). The bids submitted for the tender, numbering (2), were opened as recorded in the price schedule. The Agency's Board of Directors decided to refer the submitted bid documents to the concerned entity for study and to provide the necessary recommendations thereon within (30) days from this date. |
</table>

## Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>
<table_caption>Tender Decision for the Central Agency for Information Technology</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Statement | Subject |
|:---:|:---|:---|
| 3 | Number: - Practice 3/2024/2025 | Practice for the expansion of the Kuwait Information Network for the Central Agency for Information Technology. Decision No. (3) of Meeting No. (2025/18). The technical bids submitted for the practice, numbering (5), were opened as recorded in the price schedule. The Agency's Board of Directors decided to refer the submitted technical bid documents to the concerned entity for study and to provide the necessary recommendations thereon within (30) days from this date. |
</table>

## Abdullah Al-Salem University <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig>
### Bid Bond / Extension
<table_caption>Tender Decision for Abdullah Al-Salem University</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Statement | Subject |
|:---:|:---|:---|
| 1 | Letter No.: Letter Date: | Notification to the Agency regarding the imminent expiration of the bid bonds for companies participating in Tender No. 3/2023/2024 for operation, maintenance, and repair of engineering services in the (Al-Khaldiya - Fintas) sector. Decision No. (4) of Meeting No. (2025/18). The Agency's Board of Directors decided to request the bidders to extend the bid bonds for all companies participating in the tender, pursuant to Article No. (46) of the Public Tenders Law No. 49 of 2016. |
</table>

Auction documents can be obtained during official working hours from the Procurement Department's website: https://pur.ku.edu.kw. The complete bid, sealed with the company's stamp, must be submitted on a CD (3 copies) no later than 12:00 PM on Tuesday, 08/04/2025. Bids received after this deadline will not be considered. Bids will be opened in a public session, provided that the following are submitted:
- The original copy of the bid and undertaking form.
- An initial bid bond of 2% of the bid value.
- The original, stamped price quotation.
- A copy of a valid Certificate of National Labor Percentage.
- The envelope designated for the auction.
- The purchase receipt from the website.
- The documents requested by the university in the auction documents.

# Kuwait Fund for Arab Economic Development <orig>الصندوق الكويتي للتنمية الاقتصادية العربية</orig>

## Announcement of Tender No. (2025/17)
Renewal of licenses, technical support, and maintenance for the central primary storage system at the Fund's main and disaster recovery sites, and server licenses
" The Kuwait Fund for Arab Economic Development <orig>الصندوق الكويتي للتنمية الاقتصادية العربية</orig> announces the issuance of Tender No. (2025/17) for the renewal of licenses, technical support, and maintenance for the central primary storage system at the Fund's main and disaster recovery sites, and server licenses.
Companies and institutions specialized in this field wishing to participate in this tender may access the website of the Kuwait Fund for Arab Economic Development <orig>الصندوق الكويتي للتنمية الاقتصادية العربية</orig> (www.kuwait-fund.org) or the government's electronic portal (www.e.gov.kw) for a non-refundable fee of KWD 40/- (forty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). The deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Monday, 2025/03/24. Bids shall remain valid and may not be withdrawn for a period of (90) ninety days from the date of opening the bid envelopes. The bidder must deposit with their bid a preliminary insurance of not less than 2% of the bid value, and this insurance must be valid and in effect for the duration of the bid's validity. "

Acting Deputy Director General <orig>نائب المدير العام بالوكالة</orig>

- No practitioner will be allowed to attend the preliminary meeting unless they provide proof of having obtained the documents for this tender. This applies if Kuwait Petroleum Corporation is not notified of the names and positions of its nominated attendees at least two days before the preliminary meeting.
- A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register for classification under more than one name, nor submit more than one bid for a tender, with the exception of alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
However, a person who has a stake in separate companies, where each company is independent in its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative structure, may register themselves and each of their independent companies for classification.
The bid of a practitioner who violates this article shall be considered legally null and void.
- Any inquiries or requests related to the tender documents must be sent in writing via email no later than 10:00 AM on the day following the preliminary meeting. No requests will be considered for any reason after this deadline.
- The fee for the tender documents is non-refundable.
- The initial bid bond must be valid for the entire duration of the bid's validity (90 days from the closing date) and must be submitted in favor of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig>.
- Bids must be addressed with the tender name and number and placed in the designated bid box located at the headquarters of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> – Oil Sector Complex – Shuwaikh <orig>الشويخ</orig> – Arabian Gulf Street – (Waiting Room) – next to Gate No. (1) before the specified closing date. Any bid submitted after the specified closing time will be rejected.
- The practitioner must be registered on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries (ktendering.com.kw) and must submit a certificate proving this with the bid.
- Those wishing to participate in the tender are required to send a participation request via email to:
(purch_contracts@kpc.com.kw), attaching a single .pdf file containing the following documents in the specified order:
1. A letter addressed to Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> from the authorized signatory expressing the desire to participate, including the following company details:
  - Tender title and number.
  - Name of the person responsible for coordination between the Corporation and the practitioner.
  - Direct telephone number (mobile + landline).
  - Email address (for the individual + for the company/relevant department).
  - Fax number.
  - Company address.
2. An official letter from the authorized signatory including the following:
  - Names of persons authorized to sign on behalf of the company.
  - Their job titles.
  - Telephone numbers (mobile + landline).
  - Email addresses.
3. A copy of a valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage for non-governmental entities, issued and certified by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>.
4. A copy of the company's articles of incorporation, in addition to the latest amendment contract (if any).
5. A copy of the commercial license from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
6. A recent letter (not older than 2022) containing the signature specimen of the person authorized to sign on behalf of the company, certified by the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
7. A copy of a valid registration certificate with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.

# Kuwait Ports Authority <orig>مؤسسة الموانئ الكويتية</orig>
Announcement of Tender No. (KPA/9/2024/2025) concerning the restoration and treatment of walls and ascent beams No. (4) at the Ports Complex of the Kuwait Ports Authority <orig>مؤسسة الموانئ الكويتية</orig>
The Kuwait Ports Authority <orig>مؤسسة الموانئ الكويتية</orig> announces the aforementioned tender and invites specialized companies to submit their bids in accordance with the conditions, technical specifications, and provisions outlined in the tender documents, according to the following details:

<table_caption>Tender Schedule and Requirements for KPA Tender No. KPA/9/2024/2025</table_caption>
<table>
| | Tender Issuance Date | Closing Date | Preliminary Meeting Date | Initial Bid Bond |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| | Sunday, 23/2/2025 | Thursday, 20/3/2025 at 12:00 PM | Wednesday, 12/3/2025 at 11:00 AM, Meeting Hall – 9th Floor – Ports Complex Building, Jamal Abdel Nasser Street – Shuwaikh Administrative Area | 3,000 K.D. in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee valid for 90 days from the closing date |
| | **Location for Receiving Documents and Submitting Bids** | **Document Fee** | **Final Performance Bond** |
| | Supply Department at the Authority, 7th Floor – Room 733, Ports Complex Building – Jamal Abdel Nasser Street – Shuwaikh Administrative Area | 75 K.D. | 10% of the bid value, valid throughout the contract and maintenance period, plus three months after its completion |
</table>

1- The tender is indivisible, and the submission of alternative offers is not permitted.
2- The duration for the completion of works is (120 days), commencing from the date of the commencement order, which must be issued within 15 days from the date of signing the contract. This period is considered a mobilization period and is not included in the work completion period referred to in Article (10) of these conditions.
3- The maintenance period for the works is (365 days), commencing from the date specified in the initial acceptance certificate for the works of each work order.
4- The bidder for this tender must be a Kuwaiti national – whether an individual or a company – registered in the Commercial Register and registered with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for civil and construction works, and must provide proof thereof with a recent certificate contemporary to the year the tender was issued. The bidder's experience in the field of construction contracting as a main contractor must not be less than ten years. They must attach a schedule detailing their practical experience, supported by certified documents, records, and papers. Failure to provide such proof will result in the disqualification of the bid.
5- Practitioners shall adhere to all provisions of Law No. (49) of 2016 regarding Public Tenders and its amendments, its executive regulations issued by Decree No. 30 of 2017 and its amendments, Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> Circular No. 5 of 2020, and all applicable laws, regulations, systems, and decisions in force at the Authority and the governmental bodies regulating the works subject of the tender.
6- Documents required to purchase the tender documents: (Commercial License / Signature Authorization / Authorization to receive tender documents / Registration certificate from the Central Agency for Public Tenders, a clearance certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>).

# Petrochemical Industries Company <orig>شركة صناعة الكيماويات البترولية</orig>
## Announcement
The Higher Procurement Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation and its Oil Companies (H.P.C) <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا لمناقصات مؤسسة البترول الكويتية وشركاتها النفطية</orig>, at the request of the Petrochemical Industries Company (PIC) <orig>شركة صناعة الكيماويات البترولية</orig> - Internal Procurement Committee (I.P.C) <orig>لجنة الشراء الداخلية</orig>, announces the pre-launch of Tender No. MNA/02/2025 concerning FREIGHT FORWARDING, CUSTOM CLEARANCE & TRANSPORTATION SERVICES OF MATERIALS.
Accordingly, the Petrochemical Industries Company (PIC) <orig>شركة صناعة الكيماويات البترولية</orig> would like to draw the attention of bidders to the fact that, based on the provisions of Article (16) of the Public Tenders Law No. (49) of 2016, the aforementioned tender will be offered to the list of companies/institutions shown in the table below, numbering (18) companies/institutions, after a period of at least (30 days) from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette.
Any interested party whose name is not on this list has the right to submit an official request to participate in the tender, accompanied by supporting documents for its qualification request, addressed to the Chairman of the Higher Procurement Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation and its Subsidiaries (HPC) <orig>رئيس لجنة الشراء العليا لمناقصات مؤسسة البترول الكويتية وشركاتها التابعة</orig>, within only (30 days) starting from the day following the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette.
A fee of (250) K.D. (two hundred and fifty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) shall be collected from the contractor in consideration for studying the possibility of adding them to this limited list / or for grievance requests, by virtue of a bank deposit receipt into the company's account mentioned below:-

Account Name : Petrochemical Industries Company
Banker's Name : National Bank of Kuwait, Ahmadi Branch , Kuwait

> "A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register under more than one name at the time of classification, nor submit more than one bid in a practice, with the exception of alternative bids where the terms of the practice permit their submission. (101167), Ground Floor, Building B-1, New KOC Complex, ex- (KOC Industrial Area, Ahmadi) |

- Pursuant to the text of Article (29) of Law No. 49 of 2016 regarding Public Tenders, "A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register under more than one name for classification purposes, nor submit more than one bid in a tender. This excludes alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, where each company is independent in its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative structure, may register themselves and each of their independent companies for classification. A bid from a tenderer who violates this article shall be considered null and void by law."
- Companies / tenderers wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, or other matters must adhere to submitting them to the concerned entity at the time and place specified in the table above for the preliminary meeting (inquiries session).
- The deadline for receiving inquiries and clarifications submitted by companies is 10/4/2025. No inquiries or clarifications received after this date will be considered.
- The tenderer must deposit the fee for purchasing the tender document into the Kuwait Oil Company account mentioned below, ensuring that the tender number and the company's name are included on the purchase receipt issued by the bank. The receipt must be submitted with the bid. Bids not accompanied by a payment receipt will be excluded. In the case of electronic bid submission, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached electronically with the bid:

## Announcement
### Annual Plan for Supply, Contracting, and Services Contracts

Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> announces that in accordance with Article No. (33) and Article No. (88) of the Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016 regarding the subject of the above-mentioned announcement, the plans are published weekly on the official website of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>. Therefore, all those interested in viewing them should visit the website continuously to obtain the latest updates by following the steps below:

1- The company's website WWW.KOCKW.COM
2- Click on E-business
3- Select one of the options: Tenders (RFQ's) and Procurements (RFP's)
4- Click on Upcoming
